(5.) Linear Functions: The table shows the linear relationship between the average height in feet of trees on a tree farm and the number of years since the trees were planted.

Average Tree Height
Number of Years Since the Trees Were Planted 1 3 6 11 15
Average Height (ft) 10 24 45 80 108

What is the rate of change of the average height in feet of the trees on the farm with respect to the number of years since the trees were planted?

$ A.\;\; 14 \text{ ft/yr} \\[3ex] B.\;\; 3 \text{ ft/yr} \\[3ex] C.\;\; 7 \text{ ft/yr} \\[3ex] D.\;\; 10 \text{ ft/yr} \\[3ex] $

The rate of change of the average height in feet of the trees on the farm with respect to the number of years since the trees were planted is the slope of the function.

$ \text{Point 1: } (1, 10) \\[3ex] x_1 = 1 \\[3ex] y_1 = 10 \\[5ex] \text{Point 2: } (15, 108) \\[3ex] x_2 = 15 \\[3ex] y_2 = 108 \\[5ex] \text{slope, } m = \dfrac{y_2 - y_1}{x_2 - x_1} \\[5ex] m = \dfrac{108 - 10}{15 - 1} \\[5ex] m = \dfrac{98}{14} \\[5ex] m = 7 \\[3ex] $ The rate of change of the average height in feet of the trees on the farm with respect to the number of years since the trees were planted is 7 feet per year.
(6.) Linear Functions: What is the equation in slope–intercept form of the line that passes through the points (–4, 2) and (12, 6)?

$ A.\;\; y = 0.25x + 3 \\[3ex] B.\;\; y = 0.25x - 4.5 \\[3ex] C.\;\; y = 4x + 18 \\[3ex] D.\;\; y = 4x - 42 \\[3ex] $

$ \text{Point 1: } (-4, 2) \\[3ex] x_1 = -4 \\[3ex] y_1 = 2 \\[5ex] \text{Point 2: } (12, 6) \\[3ex] x_2 = 12 \\[3ex] y_2 = 6 \\[5ex] \text{Slope, } m = \dfrac{y_2 - y_1}{x_2 - x_1} \\[5ex] m = \dfrac{6 - 2}{12 - (-4)} \\[5ex] m = \dfrac{4}{16} \\[5ex] m = 0.25 \\[5ex] \text{Point–Slope Form} \\[3ex] y - y_1 = m(x - x_1) \\[3ex] y - 2 = 0.25[x - (-4)] \\[3ex] y - 2 = 0.25(x + 4) \\[5ex] \text{Slope–Intercept Form} \\[3ex] y = mx + b ...\text{where } b \text{ is the y-intercept} \\[3ex] y = 0.25x + 1 + 2 \\[3ex] y = 0.25x + 3 $

$ -5y = -6x + 15 \\[5ex] \text{When } y = 0 \\[3ex] -5(0) = -6x + 15 \\[3ex] 0 + 6x = 15 \\[3ex] 6x = 15 \\[3ex] x = \dfrac{15}{6} \\[5ex] x = 2.5 \\[3ex] x-\text{intercept} = (2.5, 0) \\[5ex] \text{When } x = 0 \\[3ex] -5y = -6(0) + 15 \\[3ex] -5y = 0 + 15 \\[3ex] -5y = 15 \\[3ex] y = \dfrac{15}{-5} \\[5ex] y = -3 \\[3ex] y-\text{intercept} = (0, -3) \\[3ex] $ The correct answer is Option C.

$ A.\;\; \$20,780 \\[3ex] B.\;\; \$12,800 \\[3ex] C.\;\; \$28,800 \\[3ex] D.\;\; \$20,760 \\[3ex] $

$ p(n) = 52n - 0.05n^2 \\[3ex] n = 400 \\[3ex] \implies \\[3ex] p(400) = 52(400) - 0.05(400)^2 \\[3ex] = 20800 - 8000 \\[3ex] = \$12,800 $
(9.) Exponential Functions: An exponential function is graphed on the grid.



Which function is best represented by the graph?

$ A.\;\; g(x) = 6\left(\dfrac{1}{3}\right)^x \\[5ex] B.\;\; g(x) = 6(3)^x \\[4ex] C.\;\; g(x) = 6 - \left(\dfrac{1}{3}\right)^x \\[5ex] D.\;\; g(x) = 6 - (3)^x \\[4ex] $

$ \underline{\text{Exponential Function}} \\[3ex] y = ab^x \\[3ex] y-\text{intercept} = a = \text{initial value} = 6 \\[3ex] b = \text{base} \\[5ex] \text{Point: } (1, 2) \\[3ex] x = 1 \\[3ex] y = 2 \\[3ex] 2 = 6 * b^{1} \\[3ex] 6b = 2 \\[3ex] b = \dfrac{2}{6} \\[5ex] b = \dfrac{1}{3} \\[5ex] \implies \\[3ex] y = 6\left(\dfrac{1}{3}\right)^x $
(10.) Linear Functions: What is the equation in slope–intercept form of the line that crosses the x-axis at 36 and is perpendicular to the line represented by $y = -\dfrac{4}{9}x + 5$

$ A.\;\; y = \dfrac{4}{9}x + 16 \\[5ex] B.\;\; y = \dfrac{4}{9}x - 16 \\[5ex] C.\;\; y = \dfrac{9}{4}x + 81 \\[5ex] D.\;\; y = \dfrac{9}{4}x - 81 \\[5ex] $

$ m = \text{slope} \\[3ex] \text{Slope–Intercept Form: } y = mx + b \\[3ex] \text{Point–Slope Form: } y - y_1 = m(x - x_1) \\[5ex] \underline{\text{Equation 1}} \\[3ex] y = -\dfrac{4}{9}x + 5 \\[5ex] m_1 = -\dfrac{4}{9} \\[5ex] \underline{\text{Equation 2}} \\[3ex] \text{Line 2 } \perp \text{ Line 1} \\[3ex] m_1 \cdot m_2 = -1 ...\text{The product of the slopes of two perpendicular lines is} -1 \\[3ex] m_2 = -1 \div m_1 \\[3ex] m_2 = -1 \div -\dfrac{4}{9} \\[5ex] m_2 = -1 * -\dfrac{9}{4} \\[5ex] m_2 = \dfrac{9}{4} \\[5ex] \text{Passes through the } x-{intercept } (36, 0) \\[3ex] x_1 = 36 \\[3ex] y_1 = 0 \\[5ex] \text{Point–Slope Form} \\[3ex] y - 0 = \dfrac{9}{4}(x - 36) \\[5ex] \text{Slope–Intercept Form} \\[3ex] y = \dfrac{9}{4}x - 81 $

(12.) Algebra Transformations: The graph of quadratic parent function f was transformed to create the graph of $g(x) = f(x + 2) - 5$.
Which graph best represents g?

A.

B.

C.

D.


Function Family: Quadratic Function
Parent Function: $f(x)$
$f(x) = x^2$
Vertex = (0, 0)

Transformed Function: $g(x)$
$g(x) = f(x + 2) - 5$

1st Transformation: Horizontal Shift 2 units left.
(0, 0) → (0 – 2, 0)
   → (–2, 0)

2nd Transformation: Vertical Shift 5 units down.
(–2, 0) → (–2, 0 – 5)
   → (–2, –5)
Vertex = (–2, –5)
The correct answer is Option C.
(13.) Exponents: Which expression is equivalent to $\dfrac{45m^{-6}p^2v^{12}}{15m^{-2}p^8v^{-4}}$ for all values of m, p, and v where the expression is defined?

$ A.\;\; \dfrac{3v^8}{m^8p^6} \\[5ex] B.\;\; \dfrac{3v^{16}}{m^4p^6} \\[5ex] C.\;\; \dfrac{30m^3}{p^4v^3} \\[5ex] D.\;\; \dfrac{30v^3}{m^3p^4} \\[5ex] $

$ \dfrac{45m^{-6}p^2v^{12}}{15m^{-2}p^8v^{-4}} \\[5ex] \text{DISSOCIATE} \\[3ex] \dfrac{45 \cdot m^{-6} \cdot p^2 \cdot v^{12}}{15 \cdot m^{-2} \cdot p^8 \cdot v^{-4}} \\[5ex] \dfrac{45}{15} \cdot \dfrac{m^{-6}}{m^{-2}} \cdot \dfrac{p^2}{p^8} \cdot \dfrac{v^{12}}{v^{-4}} \\[5ex] \text{SOLVE} \\[3ex] 3 \cdot m^{-6 - (-2)} \cdot p^{2 - 8} \cdot v^{12 - (-4)}...\text{Law 2 Exp} \\[4ex] 3 \cdot m^{-4} \cdot p^{-6} \cdot v^{16} \\[4ex] 3 \cdot \dfrac{1}{m^4} \cdot \dfrac{1}{p^6} \cdot v^{16} ...\text{Law 6 Exp} \\[5ex] \text{ASSOCIATE} \\[3ex] \dfrac{3v^{16}}{m^4p^6} $
(14.) Quadratic Equations: What is the positive solution to this equation? $ 4x^2 + 12x = 135 \\[3ex] $ Record your answer in the boxes below.




$ 4x^2 + 12x = 135 \\[3ex] 4x^2 + 12x - 135 = 0 \\[3ex] 4x^2 * -135 = -540x^2 \\[3ex] \text{Factors are: } 30x \text{ and } -18x \\[3ex] 4x^2 + 30x - 18x - 135 = 0 \\[3ex] 2x(2x + 15) - 9(2x + 15) = 0 \\[3ex] (2x + 15)(2x - 9) = 0 \\[3ex] \underline{\text{Zero Product Property}} \\[3ex] 2x + 15 = 0 \text{ or } 2x - 9 = 0 \\[3ex] 2x = -15 \text{ or } 2x = 9 \\[3ex] x = -\dfrac{15}{2} \text{ or } x = \dfrac{9}{2} \\[5ex] x = -7.5 \text{ or } x = 4.5 $
(15.) Linear Inequalities: A grill at a barbecue restaurant will be used to cook sausage links that are 2 lb each and briskets that are 6 lb each.
No more than 120 lb of sausage links and briskets will be cooked on the grill.
Which inequality represents all possible combinations of x, the number of sausage links that will be cooked on the grill, and y, the number of briskets that will also be cooked?

$ A.\;\; 6x + 2y \lt 120 \\[3ex] B.\;\; 2x + 6y \le 120 \\[3ex] C.\;\; 6x + 2y \gt 120 \\[3ex] D.\;\; 2x + 6y \ge 120 \\[3ex] $

x = the number of sausage links that will be cooked on the grill
y = the number of briskets

Mass
x sausage links @ 2 lb each = 2x
y briskets @ 6 lb each = 6y

Total Mass
No more than 120 lb of sausage links and briskets will be cooked on the grill.
⇒ $2x + 6y \le 120$

$ (10 + 7r - r^2) + (-6r^2 - 18 + 5r) \\[3ex] (-r^2 + 7r + 10) + (-6r^2 + 5r - 18) \\[3ex] \underline{\text{Vertical Method}} \\[3ex] \begin{array}{c} -r^2 + 7r + 10 \\ +\hspace{7em} \\ -6r^2 + 5r - 18 \\ \hline -7r^2 + 12r - 8 \\ \hline \end{array} $

A.

B.

C.

D.


Because the inequality does not contain an equal sign, the line will be a dashed line.

$ y \gt 3x - 4 \\[5ex] \text{When } x = 0 \\[3ex] y \gt 3(0) - 4 \\[3ex] y \gt 0 - 4 \\[3ex] y \gt -4 ...\text{Mark point } (0, -4) \\[3ex] \text{The shaded area is upwards from } y = -4 \\[5ex] \text{When } y = 0 \\[3ex] 0 \gt 3x - 4 \\[3ex] 3x - 4 \lt 0 \\[3ex] 3x \lt 0 + 4 \\[3ex] 3x \lt 4 \\[3ex] x \lt \dfrac{4}{3} \\[5ex] x \lt 1.3\bar{3} ...\text{Mark point } (1.3\bar{3}, 0) \\[3ex] \text{The shaded area is to the left of } x = 1.3\bar{3} \\[3ex] $ Draw a straight dashed line connecting the two points: $(0, -4)$ and $(1.3\bar{3}, 0)$

(18.) Exponential Functions: A bank account earning annual compound interest was opened, and no additional deposits or withdrawals were made after the initial deposit.
The balance in the account after x years can be modeled by $b(x) = 850(1.025)^x$.
Which statement is the best interpretation of one of the values in this function?

A. The initial balance of the account decreases at a rate of 97.5% each year.
B. The balance in the account increases at a rate of 2.5% each year.
C. The initial balance of the account was $1,025.
D. The balance in the account at the end of one year is $850.


$ \underline{\text{Exponential Function}} \\[3ex] b(x) = 850(1.025)^x \\[3ex] \text{initial value} = 850 \\[3ex] 1.025 \gt 1 ...\text{hence the function is Exponential Growth} \\[3ex] \text{growth factor} = 1.025 \\[5ex] \underline{\text{Exponential Growth Function}} \\[3ex] b(x) = 850(1 + 0.025)^x \\[3ex] \text{growth rate} = 0.025 * 100 = 2.5\% \\[3ex] $ This implies that the balance in the account increases at a rate of 2.5% each year.
(19.) Quadratic Functions: A company collected data for the number of text messages sent and received using a text-message application since October 2011.
The table shows the number of text messages sent and received in billions over time.
The data can be modeled by a quadratic function.

Text Messages
Number of Months since October 2011, t Number of Text Messages, n(t) (billions)
5 3
10 10
15 17
20 27
25 44
30 64
35 86
40 112

Which function best models the data?

$ A.\;\; n(t) = -0.002t^2 + 0.55t + 5.02 \\[3ex] B.\;\; n(t) = 0.072t^2 - 0.15t + 2.73 \\[3ex] C.\;\; n(t) = -0.002t^2 + 5.02 \\[3ex] D.\;\; n(t) = 0.072t^2 + 2.73 \\[3ex] $

There are at least two approaches to solve the question.
We can find the answer by analyzing the options.
We can also write a 3 by 3 linear system using the information given to us.
I recommend that we analyze the options to get the answer, rather than solving a 3 by 3 linear system to get the function.
Analyzing the options: let us test the first option.

$ \text{Point 1: } (5, 3) \\[3ex] t = 5 \\[3ex] n(t) = 3 \\[5ex] \text{Option A.} \\[3ex] n(5) = -0.002(5^2) + 0.55(5) + 5.02 \\[3ex] n(5) = 7.72 \ne 3 \\[3ex] \text{Discard} \\[5ex] \text{Option B.} \\[3ex] n(5) = 0.072(5^2) - 0.15(5) + 2.73 \\[3ex] n(5) = 3.78 \\[3ex] \text{Do not discard because 3.78 is close to 3} \\[5ex] \text{Option C.} \\[3ex] n(5) = -0.002(5^2) + 5.02 \\[3ex] n(5) = 4.97 \ne 3 \\[3ex] \text{Discard} \\[5ex] \text{Option D.} \\[3ex] n(5) = 0.072(5^2) + 2.73 \\[3ex] n(5) = 4.53 \ne 3 \\[3ex] \text{Discard} \\[5ex] \text{Just to confirm, test another value for Option B.} \\[3ex] \text{Point 8: } (40, 112) \\[3ex] t = 40 \\[3ex] n(t) = 112 \\[5ex] \text{Option B.} \\[3ex] n(40) = 0.072(40^2) - 0.15(40) + 2.73 \\[3ex] n(40) = 111.93 \\[3ex] 111.93 \approx 112 \\[3ex] $ Option B. is the correct answer.
(20.) Linear Functions: The graph of a linear function is shown on the grid.



What is the rate of change of y with respect to x for this function?
Record your answer in the boxes below.




The rate of change of y with respect to x for the function is the slope of the function. $ \text{Point 1: } (-3, 3.6) \\[3ex] x_1 = -3 \\[3ex] y_1 = 3.6 \\[5ex] \text{Point 2: } (5, 2) \\[3ex] x_2 = 5 \\[3ex] y_2 = 2 \\[5ex] \text{slope, } m = \dfrac{y_2 - y_1}{x_2 - x_1} \\[5ex] m = \dfrac{2 - 3.6}{5 - (-3)} \\[5ex] m = \dfrac{-1.6}{8} \\[5ex] m = -0.2 $
(21.) Quadratic Functions: Which graph best represents $y = -x^2 + 6x - 1$?

A.

B.

C.

D.


$ y = -x^2 + 6x - 1 \\[3ex] \text{Compare to the standard form of a quadratic function: } y = ax^2 + bx + c \\[3ex] a = -1 \\[3ex] b = 6 \\[3ex] c = -1 \\[3ex] $ 1st: Leading Coefficient
Leading Coefficient, a = –1
–1 < 0
The parabola (graph of a quadratic function) is concave down because the leading coefficient is negative.

2nd: Vertex

$ x-\text{coordinate of Vertex} = -\dfrac{b}{2a} \\[5ex] = -\dfrac{6}{2(-1)} \\[5ex] = \dfrac{-6}{-2} \\[5ex] = 3 \\[5ex] x-\text{coordinate of Vertex} = f(3) \\[3ex] = -1(3)^2 + 6(3) + (-1) \\[3ex] = -9 + 18 - 1 \\[3ex] = 8 \\[5ex] \text{Vertex} = (3, 8) \\[3ex] $ Option A. is the correct answer.

Based on the table, what is the best prediction of the number of clicks on the advertisement if 1,500 people visit the website?

$ A.\;\; 77 \\[3ex] B.\;\; 137 \\[3ex] C.\;\; 83 \\[3ex] D.\;\; 105 \\[3ex] $

$ \text{Point 1: } (153, 14) \\[3ex] x_1 = 153 \\[3ex] y_1 = 14 \\[5ex] \text{Point 2: } (1106, 63) \\[3ex] x_2 = 1106 \\[3ex] y_2 = 63 \\[5ex] \text{Slope, } m = \dfrac{y_2 - y_1}{x_2 - x_1} \\[5ex] m = \dfrac{63 - 14}{1106 - 153} \\[5ex] m = \dfrac{49}{953} \\[5ex] \text{Point–Slope Form} \\[3ex] y - y_1 = m(x - x_1) \\[3ex] y - 14 = \dfrac{49}{953}(x - 153) \\[5ex] y = \dfrac{49}{953}(x - 153) + 14 \\[5ex] \text{When } x = 1500 \\[3ex] y = \dfrac{49}{953}(1500 - 153) + 14 \\[5ex] y = \dfrac{49}{953} * 1347 + \dfrac{14 * 953}{953} \\[5ex] y = \dfrac{66003}{953} + \dfrac{13342}{953} \\[5ex] y = \dfrac{66003 + 13342}{953} \\[5ex] y = \dfrac{79345}{953} \\[5ex] y = 83.25813221 \approx 83...\text{to the nearest whole number} $
(23.) Linear Functions: The graph of a linear function is shown on the grid.



Which equation is best represented by this graph?

$ A.\;\; y + 2 = \dfrac{7}{5}(x + 7) \\[5ex] B.\;\; y - 2 = \dfrac{7}{5}(x - 7) \\[5ex] C.\;\; y + 2 = \dfrac{5}{7}(x + 7) \\[5ex] D.\;\; y - 2 = \dfrac{5}{7}(x - 7) \\[5ex] $

$ m = \text{slope} \\[3ex] b = y-\text{intercept} = -3 \\[5ex] \text{Point 1: } (0, -3) \\[3ex] x_1 = 0 \\[3ex] y_1 = -3 \\[5ex] \text{Point 2: } (4, 0) \\[3ex] x_2 = 4 \\[3ex] y_2 = 0 \\[5ex] m = \dfrac{y_2 - y_1}{x_2 - x_1} \\[5ex] m = \dfrac{0 - (-3)}{4 - 0} \\[5ex] m = \dfrac{3}{4} \\[5ex] \text{Slope–Intercept Form} \\[3ex] y = mx + b \\[3ex] y = \dfrac{3}{4}x - 3 \\[5ex] $ Our answer is not listed as an option.
So, let us find the answer option that best resembles our answer.

The slope is $\dfrac{3}{4} = 0.75$.
The slope should be less than 1.
Discard Options A. and B because the slope in those functions is $\dfrac{7}{5}$
Besides $\dfrac{5}{7}$ is closer to $\dfrac{3}{4}$ rather than $\dfrac{7}{5}$.

Let us simplify Options C. and D. so we can find the y-intercept for each function.

$ \text{Option C.} \\[3ex] y + 2 = \dfrac{5}{7}(x + 7) \\[5ex] y + 2 = \dfrac{5}{7}x + 5 \\[5ex] y = \dfrac{5}{7}x + 5 - 2 \\[5ex] y = \dfrac{5}{7}x + 3 \\[5ex] b = 3 \\[3ex] $ Discard Option C. because the y-intercept is 3, rather than –3.

$ \text{Option D.} \\[3ex] y - 2 = \dfrac{5}{7}(x - 7) \\[5ex] y - 2 = \dfrac{5}{7}x - 5 \\[5ex] y = \dfrac{5}{7}x - 5 + 2 \\[5ex] y = \dfrac{5}{7}x - 3 \\[5ex] b = -3 \\[3ex] $ Option D. is the correct answer.
(24.) Exponents: Which expression is equivalent to $\left(xy^{-6}\right)^2$ for all values of x and y where the expression is defined?

$ A.\;\; xy^{-36} \\[4ex] B.\;\; xy^{36} \\[4ex] C.\;\; x^2y^{-12} \\[4ex] D.\;\; x^2y^{12} \\[4ex] $

$ \left(xy^{-6}\right)^2 \\[4ex] \text{DISSCOCIATE} \\[3ex] \left(x \cdot y^{-6}\right)^2 \\[4ex] \text{SOLVE} \\[3ex] x^2 \cdot y^{-6 \cdot 2} ...\text{Law 5 Exp} \\[4ex] x^2 \cdot y^{-12} \\[4ex] \text{ASSOCIATE} \\[3ex] x^2y^{-12} $
(25.) System of Linear Equations: A college student completed some courses worth 3 credits and some courses worth 4 credits.
The student earned a total of 59 credits after completing 18 courses.
How many courses worth 3 credits did the student complete?

$ A.\;\; 13 \\[3ex] B.\;\; 5 \\[3ex] C.\;\; 20 \\[3ex] D.\;\; 39 \\[3ex] $

Let the number of:
courses worth 3 credits = p
courses worth 4 credits = k

Completed 18 courses ⇒
$p + k = 18...eqn.(1)$

p courses @ 3 credits each = 3p
k courses @ 4 credits each = 4k

Earned a total of 59 credits ⇒
$3p + 4k = 59...eqn.(1)$

$ p + k = 18...eqn.(1) \\[3ex] 3p + 4k = 59...eqn.(2) \\[3ex] \underline{\text{Substitution Method}} \\[3ex] \text{From } eqn.(1) \\[3ex] k = 18 - p \\[3ex] \text{Substitute for } k \text{ in } eqn.(2) \\[3ex] 3p + 4(18 - p) = 59 \\[3ex] 3p + 72 - 4p = 59 \\[3ex] 72 - 59 = 4p - 3p \\[3ex] 13 = p \\[3ex] p = 13 \\[3ex] $ The college student completed 13 courses worth 3 credits.
(26.) Linear Functions: The graph of linear function f passes through the point (1, –9) and has a slope of –3.



What is the zero of f?

$ A.\;\; 2 \\[3ex] B.\;\; 4 \\[3ex] C.\;\; -6 \\[3ex] D.\;\; -2 \\[3ex] $

$ m = \text{slope} = -3 \\[5ex] \text{Passes through Point } (1, -9) \\[3ex] x_1 = 1 \\[3ex] y_1 = -9 \\[5ex] \text{Point–Slope Form} \\[3ex] y - y_1 = m(x - x_1) \\[3ex] y - (-9) = -3(x - 1) \\[3ex] y + 9 = -3x + 3 \\[3ex] y = -3x + 3 - 9 \\[3ex] y = -3x - 6 \\[3ex] -3x - 6 = y \\[5ex] \text{Zero of } f \\[3ex] \text{When } y = 0 \\[3ex] -3x - 6 = 0 \\[3ex] -3x = 0 + 6 \\[3ex] -3x = 6 \\[3ex] x = \dfrac{6}{-3} \\[5ex] x = -2 $

Record your answer in the boxes below.




$ h(x) = 29(5.2)^x \\[3ex] y-\text{intercept} = h(0) \\[3ex] h(0) = 29(5.2)^0 \\[3ex] h(0) = 29(1)...\text{Law 3 Exp} \\[3ex] h(0) = 29 $
(28.) Quadratic Functions: The graph of a quadratic function is shown on the grid.



Which function is best represented by this graph?

$ A.\;\; h(x) = x^2 - 3x - 9 \\[3ex] B.\;\; h(x) = x^2 + 3x - 9 \\[3ex] C.\;\; h(x) = x^2 - 6x \\[3ex] D.\;\; h(x) = x^2 + 6x \\[3ex] $

We can solve the question using at least two approaches.
Use any approach you prefer.

$ a = \text{leading coefficient} \\[5ex] \underline{\text{1st Approach: Equation of a Quadratic Function in Factored Form}} \\[3ex] f(x) = a(x - \alpha)(x - \beta) \\[3ex] \alpha, \beta = \text{zeros of the function} \\[3ex] \alpha = 0 \\[3ex] \beta = 6 \\[5ex] \implies \\[3ex] h(x) = a(x - 0)(x - 6) \\[3ex] h(x) = ax(x - 6) \\[5ex] \text{Passes through the point (vertex) } (3, -9) \\[3ex] x = 3 \\[3ex] h(x) = -9 \\[3ex] \implies \\[3ex] -9 = a(3)(3 - 6) \\[3ex] -9 = a(3)(-3) \\[3ex] -9 = -9a \\[3ex] -9a = -9 \\[3ex] a = \dfrac{-9}{-9} = 1 \\[5ex] \implies \\[3ex] h(x) = 1 * x(x - 6) \\[3ex] h(x) = x(x - 6) \\[3ex] h(x) = x^2 - 6x \\[5ex] \underline{\text{2nd Approach: Equation of a Quadratic Function in Vertex Form}} \\[3ex] h(x) = a(x - h)^2 + k ...\text{where } (h, k) \text{ is the vertex} \\[3ex] (h, k) = (3, -9) \\[3ex] h = 3 \\[3ex] k = -9 \\[3ex] \implies \\[3ex] h(x) = a(x - 3)^2 + (-9) \\[3ex] h(x) = a(x - 3)^2 - 9 \\[5ex] \text{Passes through the point: } (6, 0) \\[3ex] x = 6 \\[3ex] h(x) = 0 \\[3ex] \implies \\[3ex] 0 = a(6 - 3)^2 - 9 \\[3ex] 0 = a(3)^2 - 9 \\[3ex] 0 = 9a - 9 \\[3ex] 9 = 9a \\[3ex] 9a = 9 \\[3ex] a = \dfrac{9}{9} \\[5ex] a = 1 \\[3ex] \implies \\[3ex] h(x) = a(x - 3)^2 - 9 \\[3ex] h(x) = (x - 3)(x - 3) - 9 \\[3ex] h(x) = x^2 - 3x - 3x + 9 - 9 \\[3ex] h(x) = x^2 - 6x $
(29.) Factoring: Which expressions is equivalent to $24x^2 - 22x + 5$?

$ A.\;\; (12x + 5)(2x + 1) \\[3ex] B.\;\; (8x - 5)(3x - 1) \\[3ex] C.\;\; (12x - 5)(2x - 1) \\[3ex] D.\;\; (8x + 5)(3x + 1) \\[3ex] $

$ 24x^2 - 22x + 5 \\[3ex] 24x^2 * 5 = 120x^2 \\[3ex] \text{Factors are: } -10x \text{ and } -12x \\[3ex] \implies \\[3ex] 24x^2 - 12x - 10x + 5 \\[3ex] 12x(2x - 1) - 5(2x - 1) \\[3ex] (2x - 1)(12x - 5) $
(30.) System of Linear Equations: A system of equations is graphed on the grid.



Which system of equations does the graph represent?

$ A.\;\; y = -x - 4 \\[3ex] \hspace{1.6em} y = 2x - 2 \\[5ex] B.\;\; y = -x + 4 \\[3ex] \hspace{1.6em} y = 2x - 4 \\[5ex] C.\;\; y = x - 4 \\[3ex] \hspace{1.6em} y = -2x - 2 \\[5ex] D.\;\; y = x + 4 \\[3ex] \hspace{1.6em} y = -2x - 4 \\[3ex] $

$ m = \text{slope} \\[3ex] b = y-\text{intercept} \\[3ex] y - y_1 = m(x - x_1)...\text{Point–Slope Form} \\[3ex] y = mx + b ...\text{Slope–Intercept Form} \\[5ex] \underline{\text{Line with the positive slope}} \\[3ex] \text{Point 1: } (-1, 3) \\[3ex] x_1 = -1 \\[3ex] y_1 = 3 \\[5ex] \text{Point 2: } (1, 5) \\[3ex] x_2 = 1 \\[3ex] y_2 = 5 \\[5ex] m = \dfrac{y_2 - y_1}{x_2 - x_1} \\[5ex] m = \dfrac{5 - 3}{1 - (-1)} \\[5ex] m = \dfrac{2}{2} \\[5ex] m = 1 \\[5ex] \text{Point–Slope Form} \\[3ex] y - 3 = 1(x - (-1)) \\[3ex] y - 3 = x + 1 \\[5ex] \text{Slope–Intercept Form} \\[3ex] y = x + 1 + 3 \\[3ex] y = x + 4 \\[5ex] \underline{\text{Line with the negative slope}} \\[3ex] \text{Point 1: } (-4, 4) \\[3ex] x_1 = -4 \\[3ex] y_1 = 4 \\[5ex] \text{Point 2: } (5, -3) \\[3ex] x_2 = -1 \\[3ex] y_2 = -2 \\[5ex] m = \dfrac{y_2 - y_1}{x_2 - x_1} \\[5ex] m = \dfrac{-2 - 4}{-1 - (-4)} \\[5ex] m = -\dfrac{-6}{3} \\[5ex] m = -2 \\[5ex] \text{Point–Slope Form} \\[3ex] y - 4 = -2[x - (-4)] \\[3ex] y - 4 = -2(x + 4) \\[3ex] y - 4 = -2x - 8 \\[5ex] \text{Slope–Intercept Form} \\[3ex] y = -2x - 8 + 4 \\[3ex] y = -2x - 4 \\[5ex] \therefore \text{The system of equations shown on the graph is:} \\[3ex] y = x + 4 \\[3ex] y = -2x - 4 $

$ m = \text{slope} \\[3ex] \text{Point–Slope Form: } y - y_1 = m(x - x_1) \\[3ex] \text{Slope–Intercept Form: } y = mx + b \\[3ex] x = n \\[3ex] y = f(n) \\[5ex] \text{Point 1: } (1, 21) \\[3ex] x_1 = 1 \\[3ex] y_1 = 21 \\[5ex] \text{Point 2: } (7, 3) \\[3ex] x_2 = 7 \\[3ex] y_2 = 3 \\[5ex] m = \dfrac{y_2 - y_1}{x_2 - x_1} \\[5ex] m = \dfrac{3 - 21}{7 - 1} \\[5ex] m = \dfrac{-18}{6} \\[5ex] m = -3 \\[5ex] \text{Point–Slope Form} \\[3ex] y - 21 = -3(x - 1) \\[3ex] y - 21 = -3x + 3 \\[3ex] \text{Slope–Intercept Form} \\[3ex] y = -3x + 3 + 21 \\[3ex] y = -3x + 24 \\[3ex] \implies \\[3ex] f(n) = -3n + 24 $
(33.) Algebra Transformations: The graph of $f(x) = x^2$ was transformed to create the graph of $g(x) = f(x) -9$.
Which statement about the graphs is true?

A. The graph of g is a reflection of the graph of f across the x-axis.
B. The vertex of the graph of g is 9 units to the right of the vertex of the graph of f.
C. The graph of g is a reflection of the graph of f across the y-axis.
D. The y-intercept of the graph of g is 9 units below the y-intercept of the graph of f.


Parent Function

$ f(x) = x^2 \\[3ex] \text{Vertex} = y-\text{intercept} = (0, 0)...\text{uniquely for this function} \\[3ex] $ Child Function

$ g(x) = f(x) - 9 \\[3ex] g(x) = x^2 - 9 \\[3ex] $ Transformation done to Parent to Give Child
Vertical Shift 9 units down.

$ (0, 0) \rightarrow (0, 0 - 9) \\[3ex] \hspace{2.5em} \rightarrow (0, -9) \\[3ex] $ So, the y-intercept of the graph of g is 9 units below the y-intercept of the graph of f.
(34.) Exponents: The exponent $\left(x^{22}\right)\left(x^7\right)^3$ is equivalent to $x^p$.
What is the value of p?
Record your answer in the boxes below.




$ x^p = \left(x^{22}\right)\left(x^7\right)^3 \\[4ex] \text{DISSOCIATE} \\[3ex] = x^{22} \cdot (x^7)^3 \\[4ex] = \text{SOLVE} \\[3ex] = x^{22} \cdot x^{7 \cdot 3} ...\text{Law 5 Exp} \\[4ex] = x^{22} \cdot x^{21} \\[4ex] = x^{22 + 21} ...\text{Law 1 Exp} \\[4ex] = x^{43} \\[4ex] \implies \\[3ex] x^p = x^{43} \\[4ex] \text{Same base; equate exponents} \\[3ex] p = 43 $
(35.) Linear Functions: The graph of linear function k passes through the points (–7, 0) and (1, 8).



Which statement must be true?

A. The slope of the graph of k is $-\dfrac{4}{3}$.
B. The graph of k passes through the point (–1, –8).
C. The zero of k is 7.
D. The x-intercept of the graph of k is –7.


Let us analyze each option.

$ \text{Point 1: } (-7, 0) \\[3ex] x_1 = -7 \\[3ex] y_1 = 0 \\[5ex] \text{Point 2: } (1, 8) \\[3ex] x_2 = 1 \\[3ex] y_2 = 8 \\[5ex] \text{Slope, } m = \dfrac{y_2 - y_1}{x_2 - x_1} \\[5ex] m = \dfrac{8 - 0}{1 - (-7)} \\[5ex] m = \dfrac{8}{8} \\[5ex] m = 1 \\[3ex] $ Optioan A. is incorrect.
Discard.

$ \text{Point–Slope Form and } \text{Slope–Intercept Form} \\[3ex] y - y_1 = m(x - x_1) \\[3ex] y - 0 = 1[x - (-7)] \\[3ex] y = x + 7 \\[5ex] \text{For } (-1, -8) \\[3ex] x = -1 \\[3ex] y = -8 \\[3ex] -8 \stackrel{?}{=} -1 + 7 \\[3ex] -8 \ne 6 \\[3ex] $ Optioan B. is incorrect.
Discard.

$ y = x + 7 \\[3ex] \text{When } y = 0 \\[3ex] 0 = x + 7 \\[3ex] x + 7 = 0 \\[3ex] x = -7 \\[3ex] x-\text{intercept} = (-7, 0) \\[3ex] $ Optioan C. is incorrect.
The zero of k is –7.
Discard.

Optioan D. is the correct answer.
The x-intercept of the graph of k is –7.

(40.) Quadratic Equations: Which value of x is a solution to this equation?

$ 5x^2 - 36x + 36 = 0 \\[5ex] A.\;\; x = -6 \\[3ex] B.\;\; x = 4 \\[3ex] C.\;\; x = -1.8 \\[3ex] D.\;\; x = 1.2 \\[3ex] $

$ 5x^2 - 36x + 36 = 0 \\[3ex] 5x^2 * 36 = 180x^2 \\[3ex] \text{Factors are: } -30x \text{ and } -6x \\[3ex] \implies \\[3ex] 5x^2 - 30x - 6x + 36 = 0 \\[3ex] 5x(x - 6) - 6(x - 6) = 0 \\[3ex] (x - 6)(5x - 6) = 0 \\[3ex] x - 6 = 0 \text{ or } 5x - 6 = 0...\text{Zero Product Property} \\[3ex] x = 6 \\[3ex] \text{ or } \\[3ex] 5x = 6 \\[3ex] x = \dfrac{6}{5} \\[5ex] x = 1.2 $
(41.) Exponential Functions: A part of an exponential function is graphed on the grid.



Which inequality best represents the domain of the part shown?

$ A.\;\; x \ge -2 \\[3ex] B.\;\; y \ge 4.5 \\[3ex] C.\;\; x \ge 4.5 \\[3ex] D.\;\; y \ge -2 \\[3ex] $

The domain is the set of all the input values, x for which the function has an output.
The closed circle represents a closed interval. It shows that the end point is included.
On the graph, it is on the left hand side at x = –2

The arrow represents infinity
On the graph, it is on the right hand side.
It represents positive infinity.

So, the interval notation is: $[-2, \infty)$
This represents all real numbers greater than or equal to –2.
$x \ge -2$

(43.) Quadratic Functions: Which function is equivalent to $y = 3(x + 2)^2 + 7$?

$ A.\;\; y = 3x^2 + 12x + 33 \\[3ex] B.\;\; y = 3x^2 + 12x + 19 \\[3ex] C.\;\; y = 3x^2 + 19 \\[3ex] D.\;\; y = 3x^2 + 33 \\[3ex] $

There are at least two approaches that we can use to solve the question.
Use any approach you prefer.

$ \text{1st Approach: Expansion} \\[3ex] y = 3(x + 2)^2 + 7 \\[3ex] = 3[(x + 2)(x + 2)] + 7 \\[3ex] = 3(x^2 + 2x + 2x + 4) + 7 \\[3ex] = 3(x^2 + 4x + 4) + 7 \\[3ex] = 3x^2 + 12x + 12 + 7 \\[3ex] = 3x^2 + 12x + 19 \\[5ex] \text{2nd Approach: Conversion} \\[3ex] y = 3(x + 2)^2 + 7 \\[3ex] \text{Compare to: } y = a(x - h)^2 + k ...\text{Quadratic Function in Vertex Form} \\[3ex] a = 3 \\[3ex] -h = 2 \implies h = -2 \\[3ex] k = 7 \\[3ex] \text{Vertex} = (h, k) = (-2, 7) \\[3ex] x-\text{coordinate of Vertex} = -2 \\[3ex] y-\text{coordinate of Vertex} = 7 \\[5ex] \text{Also} \\[3ex] x-\text{coordinate of Vertex} = -\dfrac{b}{2a} \\[5ex] \implies \\[3ex] -\dfrac{b}{2a} = -2 \\[5ex] \dfrac{b}{2(3)} = 2 \\[5ex] \dfrac{b}{6} = 2 \\[5ex] b = 6(2) \\[3ex] b = 12 \\[5ex] \text{Also} \\[3ex] y-\text{coordinate of Vertex} = \dfrac{4ac - b^2}{4a} \\[5ex] \implies \\[3ex] \dfrac{4ac - b^2}{4a} = 7 \\[5ex] \dfrac{4 \cdot 3 \cdot c - 12^2}{4 \cdot 3} = 7 \\[5ex] \dfrac{12c - 144}{12} = 7 \\[5ex] 12c - 144 = 12 \cdot 7 \\[3ex] 12c = 84 + 144 \\[3ex] 12c = 228 \\[3ex] c = \dfrac{228}{12} \\[5ex] c = 19 \\[5ex] \text{Convert to: } y = ax^2 + bx + c ...\text{Quadratic Function in Standard Form} \\[3ex] y = 3x^2 + 12x + 19 $
(44.) Relations and Functions: Which table shows y as a function of x?

A.
x –13 –13 –13 –13
y –2 0 5 7


B.
x –6 –1 –1 10
y 3 –1 5 –9


C.
x 1 3 7 12
y 4 4 4 4


D.
x –9 –2 0 0
y –7 –5 0 6



A function is a relation in which each input has a unique output.
This means that an input can have only one output, two inputs can have the same output, however, an input cannot have more than one output.

Let us analyze each option and discard the incorrect ones.
Option A.
The input, –13 has more than one output.
This is not a function.
Discard.

Option B.
The input, –1 has more than one output.
This is not a function.
Discard.

Option C.
All the input has the same output.
Two or more people can make the same grade on an exam, however, one person cannot make two different grades on the same exam.
This is a function.
Option C. is the correct answer.

Option D.
The input, 0 has more than one output.
This is not a function.
Discard.
(45.) Linear Functions: What is the equation in slope–intercept form of the line that passes through the point (5, 0) and is parallel to the line represented by $y = 1.2x + 3.8$?

$ A.\;\; y = 1.2x - 6 \\[3ex] B.\;\; y = -1.2x + 6 \\[3ex] C.\;\; y = 1.2x + 5 \\[3ex] D.\;\; y = -1.2x - 5 \\[3ex] $

$ m = \text{slope} \\[3ex] b = y-\text{intercept} \\[3ex] \text{Point–Slope Form: } y - y_1 = m(x - x_1) \\[3ex] \text{Slope–Intercept Form: } y = mx + b \\[5ex] \underline{\text{Line 1}} \\[3ex] y = 1.2x + 3.8 \\[3ex] m_1 = 1.2 \\[5ex] \underline{\text{Line 2}} \\[3ex] \text{Line 2 } || \text{ Line 1} \\[3ex] m_2 = m_1 = 1.2 ...\text{Parallel lines have the same slope} \\[5ex] \text{Passes through the point } (5, 0) \\[3ex] x_1 = 5 \\[3ex] y_1 = 0 \\[5ex] \text{Point–Slope Form} \\[3ex] y - 0 = 1.2(x - 5) \\[3ex] y = 1.2x - 6 $

(47.) Linear Inequalities A college student has two different jobs.
Her combined work schedules consist of no more than 48 hours in one week.
Which graph best represents the solution set for all possible combinations of x, the number of hours she worked at her first job, and y, the number of hours she worked at her second job, in one week?

A.

B.

C.

D.


In one week:
x = the number of hours she worked at her first job
y = the number of hours she worked at her second job

Her combined work schedules consist of no more than 48 hours in one week.
⇒ $x + y \le 48$
Because of the equality sign included in the inequality sign, the line drawn will be a solid line.

$ x + y \le 48 \\[5ex] \text{When } x = 0 \\[3ex] 0 + y \le 48 \\[3ex] y \le 48 ...\text{Mark point } (0, 48) \\[3ex] \text{The shaded area is downwards from } y = 48 \\[5ex] \text{When } y = 0 \\[3ex] x + 0 \le 48 \\[3ex] x \le 48 ...\text{Mark point } (48, 0) \\[3ex] \text{The shaded area is to the left of } x = 48 \\[3ex] $ Draw a straight solid line connecting the two points: $(0, 48)$ and $(48, 0)$
Shade the regions accordingly.
Locate the overlap of the two regions.
The correct answer is Option A.
(48.) Factoring: Which function is equivalent to $q(x) = 9x^2 - 24x + 16$

$ A.\;\; q(x) = (9x - 4)(x - 4) \\[3ex] B.\;\; q(x) = (3x + 4)^2 \\[3ex] C.\;\; q(x) = (9x + 4)(x + 4) \\[3ex] D.\;\; q(x) = (3x - 4)^2 \\[3ex] $

$ q(x) = 9x^2 - 24x + 16 \\[3ex] 9x^2 * 16 = 144x^2 \\[3ex] \text{Factors are: } -12x \text{ and } -12x \\[3ex] \implies \\[3ex] q(x) = 9x^2 - 12x - 12x + 16 \\[3ex] = 3x(3x - 4) - 4(3x - 4) \\[3ex] = (3x - 4)(3x - 4) \\[3ex] = (3x - 4)^2 $
(49.) System of Linear Equations: Which graph best represents this system of equations and its solution?

$ 8x - 4y = -16 \\[3ex] 3x + 15y = -6 \\[3ex] $ A.

B.

C.

D.


$ \text{Equation 1} \\[3ex] 8x - 4y = -16 \\[3ex] \text{When } x = 0 \\[3ex] 8(0) - 4y = -16 \\[3ex] -4y = -16 \\[3ex] y = \dfrac{-16}{-4} \\[5ex] y = 4 \\[3ex] (x, y) = (0, 4) \\[5ex] \text{When } y = 0 \\[3ex] 8x - 4(0) = -16 \\[3ex] 8x = -16 \\[3ex] x = -\dfrac{16}{8} \\[5ex] x = -2 \\[3ex] (x, y) = (-2, 0) \\[5ex] \text{Equation 2} \\[3ex] 3x + 15y = -6 \\[3ex] \text{When } x = 3 \\[3ex] 3(3) + 15y = -6 \\[3ex] 9 + 15y = -6 \\[3ex] 15y = -6 - 9 \\[3ex] 15y = -15 \\[3ex] y = -\dfrac{15}{15} \\[5ex] y = -1 \\[3ex] (x, y) = (3, -1) \\[5ex] \text{When } y = 0 \\[3ex] 3x + 15(0) = -6 \\[3ex] 3x = -6 \\[3ex] x = -\dfrac{6}{3} \\[5ex] x = -2 \\[3ex] (x, y) = (-2, 0) \\[3ex] $ The correct answer is Option B.
(50.) Relations and Functions: What are the domain and range of $g(x) -\dfrac{1}{4}(x - 17)^2 + 61$

A. Domain: All real numbers
  Range: $g(x) \le 61$

B. Domain: $x \le 17$
  Range: $g(x) \le 61$

C. Domain: All real numbers
  Range: $x \le 17$

D. Domain: $g(x) \ge 61$
  Range: $x \le 17$


The domain is the set of all real numbers.
This is because evry input, x will give a unique output, g(x).

The range is the set of all the output values, y produced by the input values of the function.
To determine the range, we need to know the:
(a.) Leading Coefficient, a
(b.) y-coordinate of the Vertex

$ g(x) -\dfrac{1}{4}(x - 17)^2 + 61 \\[5ex] \text{Compare to: } g(x) = a(x - h)^2 + k \\[4ex] \text{where } \\[3ex] a = \text{leading coefficient} = -\dfrac{1}{4} \\[5ex] k = y-\text{coordinate of the vertex} = 61 \\[3ex] $ (a.) The leading coefficient is negative.
Hence, the parabola has a maximum value.

(b.) The y-coordinate of the vertex is 61. This implies that the parabola has a maximum value of 61.

Option A. is the correct answer. A. Domain: All real numbers
  Range: $g(x) \le 61$

(51.) System of Linear Equations: A customer at a store paid $64 for 3 large candles and 4 small candles.
At the same store, a second customer paid $4 more than the first customer for 1 large candle and 8 small candles.
The price of each large candle is the same, and the price of each small candle is the same.
Which system of equations can be used to find the price in dollars of each large candle, x, and each small candle, y?

$ A.\;\; 4y = 3x + 64 \\[3ex] \hspace{1.6em} 8y = x + 68 \\[5ex] B.\;\; 4y = 3x + 64 \\[3ex] \hspace{1.6em} 8y = x + 60 \\[5ex] C.\;\; 3x + 4y = 64 \\[3ex] \hspace{1.6em} x + 8y = 68 \\[5ex] D.\;\; 3x + 4y = 64 \\[3ex] \hspace{1.6em} x + 8y = 60 \\[3ex] $

x = price in dollars of each large candle
y = price in dollars of each small candle

price for 3 large candles @ $x per large candle = $3x$
price for 4 small candles @ $y per small candle = $4y$
A customer at a store paid $64 for 3 large candles and 4 small candles.
This implies that: $3x + 4y = 64...eqn.(1)$

price for 1 large candle @ $x per large candle = $x$
price for 8 small candles @ $y per small candle = $8y$
$4 more than the first customer = 4 + 64 = $68
At the same store, a second customer paid $4 more than the first customer for 1 large candle and 8 small candles.
This implies that: $x + 8y = 68...eqn.(2)$

Parent Function: $f(x) = x$
Origin = (0, 0)
Another Point = (3, 3)

Child Function: $h(x) = -f(x) + 3$

1st Transformation: Vertical Reflection

$ (0, 0) \rightarrow (0, –0) \rightarrow (0, 0) \\[3ex] (3, 3) \rightarrow (3, –3) \\[3ex] $ 2nd Transformation: Vertical Shift 3 units up

$ (0, 0) \rightarrow (0, 0 + 3) \\[3ex] \hspace{2em} \rightarrow (0, 3) \\[5ex] (3, –3) \rightarrow (3, -3 + 3) \\[3ex] \hspace{2em} \rightarrow (3, 0) \\[3ex] $ Can we locate these points (0, 3) and (3 0) on the graph of the transformation?
The correct answer is Option B.

(54.) Variations: The total distance in centimeters a toy robot moves varies directly with the time in seconds.
The toy robot moves a total distance of 264 centimeters in 11 seconds.
What is the time in seconds the toy robot moves when the total distance is 408 centimeters?

$ A.\;\; 24\;s \\[3ex] B.\;\; 17\;s \\[3ex] C.\;\; 13\;s \\[3ex] D.\;\; 37\;s \\[3ex] $

Let the:
total distance in centimeters = d
time in seconds = t

$ d \propto t \\[3ex] d = kt ...k\text{ is the constant of variation} \\[3ex] kt = d \\[5ex] k = \dfrac{d}{t} \\[5ex] \text{When } d = 264\;cm, \;\; t = 11\;s \\[3ex] k = ? \\[3ex] k = \dfrac{264}{11} \\[5ex] k = 24\;cm/s \\[3ex] \implies \\[3ex] d = 24t \\[5ex] \text{When } d = 408\;cm, \;\; t = ? \\[3ex] 408 = 24t \\[3ex] 24t = 408 \\[3ex] t = \dfrac{408}{24} \\[5ex] t = 17\;s $

(1.) Linear Functions: At a restaurant, jars of tomato sauce are stored in boxes in the pantry.
Each box contains 8 jars of tomato sauce.
A cook uses 2 jars from 1 of the boxes.
Which function shows the relationship between y, the total number of jars of tomato sauce remaining in the pantry, and x, the number of boxes in the pantry?

$ A.\;\; y = 8x + 6 \\[3ex] B.\;\; y = 8x \\[3ex] C.\;\; y = 8x - 2 \\[3ex] D.\;\; y = 6x \\[3ex] $

y = the total number of jars of tomato sauce remaining in the pantry
x = the number of boxes in the pantry

x boxes @ 8 jars per box = $8x$ jars

A cook uses 2 jars from 1 of the boxes.
⇒ $8x - 2$ jars

∴ the total number of jars of tomato sauce remaining in the pantry, $y = 8x - 2$

(4.) Exponential Functions: Which statement about the graph of $y = 8(0.25)^x$ is true?

B. The coordinates of the y-intercept are (0, 8).
C. The equation of the asymptote is $x = 0$.
D. The graph includes the point (2, 1).


$ y-\text{intercept} \\[3ex] y = 8(0.25)^x \\[3ex] \text{When } x = 0 \\[3ex] y = 8(0.25)^0 \\[3ex] y = 8(1) ...\text{Law 3 Exp} \\[3ex] y = 8 \\[3ex] $ The y-intercept is (0, 8)

Student: SamDom For Peace
Teacher: That's my name
Student: Could you analyze all the options?
Teacher: Sure, let's do it.

$ \text{Option A.} \\[3ex] x-\text{intercept} \\[3ex] y = 8(0.25)^x \\[3ex] \text{When } y = 0 \\[3ex] 0 = 8(0.25)^x \\[3ex] 8(0.25)^x = 0 \\[3ex] 0.25^x = \dfrac{0}{8} \\[5ex] 0.25^x = 0 \\[3ex] \log 0.25^x = \log 0 \\[3ex] \log 0 \text{ DNE} \\[3ex] \text{Discard} \\[5ex] \text{Option C.} \\[3ex] \text{As } x \to \infty, \\[3ex] y = 8(0.25)^{\infty} \\[3ex] y = 8\left(\dfrac{1}{4}\right)^{\infty} \\[5ex] y = 8(0) \\[3ex] y = 0 \\[5ex] \text{As } x \to -\infty, \\[3ex] y = 8\left(\dfrac{1}{4}\right)^{-\infty} \\[5ex] y = 8\left(\dfrac{1}{4}\right)^\infty ...\text{Law 6 Exp} \\[5ex] y = 8(\infty) \\[3ex] y = \infty \\[3ex] $ Because ∞ is not a value, the horizontal asymptote is: $y = 0$
So, the equation of the asymptote is $y = 0$.
Discard.

(5.) Quadratic Functions: What is the range of $y = -x^2 - 2x + 3$?

$ A.\;\; x \le 4 \\[3ex] B.\;\; x \ge -4 \\[3ex] C.\;\; y \le 4 \\[3ex] D.\;\; y \ge -4 \\[3ex] $

$ y = -x^2 - 2x + 3 \\[3ex] \text{Compare to the standard form: } y = ax^2 + bx + c \\[5ex] \text{Leading Coefficient, } a \\[3ex] a = -1 \\[3ex] \text{Because } a \lt 0, \text{ the parabola has a maximum value.} \\[5ex] b = -2 \\[3ex] \text{Vertex} \\[3ex] \text{x-coordinate of the vertex} = -\dfrac{b}{2a} \\[5ex] = -\dfrac{-2}{2(-1)} \\[5ex] = -1 \\[5ex] \text{y-coordinate of the vertex} = f(-1) \\[3ex] = -(-1)^2 - 2(-1) + 3 \\[3ex] = -1 + 2 + 3 \\[3ex] = 4 \\[3ex] $ The range of the function is $y \le 4$.
(6.) Exponents: Which expression is equivalent to $\left(144k^2r^{14}\right)^{\dfrac{1}{2}}$ for all positive values of k and r?

$ A.\;\; 12kr^7 \\[4ex] B.\;\; 72k^2r^{14} \\[4ex] C.\;\; 144kr^7 \\[4ex] D.\;\; 12k^2r^{14} \\[4ex] $

$ \left(144k^2r^{14}\right)^{\dfrac{1}{2}} \\[4ex] \text{DISSOCIATE} \\[3ex] \left(144 \cdot k^2 \cdot r^{14}\right)^{\dfrac{1}{2}} \\[4ex] \text{SOLVE} \\[3ex] 144^{\dfrac{1}{2}} \cdot k^{2 \cdot \dfrac{1}{2}} \cdot r^{14 \cdot \dfrac{1}{2}}...\text{Law 5 Exp} \\[7ex] \sqrt{144} \cdot k^1 \cdot r^7 ...\text{Law 7 Exp} \\[4ex] 12 \cdot k \cdot r^7 \\[4ex] \text{ASSOCIATE} \\[3ex] 12kr^7 $
(7.) Quadratic Functions: The graph shows the height in feet of an object above the ground t seconds after it was launched from the ground.



Which function is best represented by the graph of this situation?

$ A.\;\; h(t) = -16t^2 - 64t \\[3ex] B.\;\; h(t) = -16t^2 + 128t - 256 \\[3ex] C.\;\; h(t) = -16t^2 + 64t \\[3ex] D.\;\; h(t) = -16t^2 - 128t - 256 \\[3ex] $

We can solve the question using at least two approaches.
Use any approach you prefer.

$ \text{Let}: \\[3ex] h(t) = f(x) \\[3ex] t = x \\[3ex] a = \text{leading coefficient} \\[5ex] \underline{\text{1st Approach: Equation of a Quadratic Function in Factored Form}} \\[3ex] f(x) = a(x - \alpha)(x - \beta) \\[3ex] \alpha, \beta = \text{zeros of the function} \\[3ex] \alpha = 0 \\[3ex] \beta = 4 \\[3ex] \implies \\[3ex] f(x) = a(x - 0)(x - 4) \\[3ex] f(x) = a(x)(x - 4) \\[5ex] \text{Passes through the point (vertex) } (2, 64) \\[3ex] x = 2 \\[3ex] f(x) = 64 \\[3ex] \implies \\[3ex] 64 = a(2)(2 - 4) \\[3ex] 64 = a(2)(-2) \\[3ex] 64 = -4a \\[3ex] -4a = 64 \\[3ex] a = \dfrac{64}{-4} \\[5ex] a = -16 \\[5ex] \implies \\[3ex] f(x) = -16(x)(x - 4) \\[3ex] f(x) = -16x(x - 4) \\[3ex] f(x) = -16x^2 + 64x \\[3ex] \implies \\[3ex] h(t) = -16t^2 + 64t \\[5ex] \underline{\text{2nd Approach: Equation of a Quadratic Function in Vertex Form}} \\[3ex] f(x) = a(x - h)^2 + k ...\text{where } (h, k) \text{ is the vertex} \\[3ex] (h, k) = (2, 64) \\[3ex] h = 2 \\[3ex] k = 64 \\[3ex] \implies \\[3ex] f(x) = a(x - 2)^2 + 64 \\[5ex] \text{Passes through the point: } (4, 0) \\[3ex] x = 4 \\[3ex] f(x) = 0 \\[3ex] \implies \\[3ex] 0 = a(4 - 2)^2 + 64 \\[3ex] 0 - 64 = a(2)^2 \\[3ex] -64 = 4a \\[3ex] 4a = -64 \\[3ex] a = \dfrac{-64}{4} \\[5ex] a = -16 \\[5ex] \implies \\[3ex] f(x) = -16(x - 2)^2 + 64 \\[3ex] f(x) = -16[(x - 2)(x - 2)] + 64 \\[3ex] f(x) = -16(x^2 - 2x - 2x + 4) + 64 \\[3ex] f(x) = -16(x^2 - 4x + 4) + 64 \\[3ex] f(x) = -16x^2 + 64x - 64 + 64 \\[3ex] f(x) = -16x^2 + 64x \\[3ex] \implies \\[3ex] h(t) = -16t^2 + 64t $

$ A.\;\; 3 \\[3ex] B.\;\; -9 \\[3ex] C.\;\; 0 \\[3ex] D.\;\; -15 \\[3ex] $

(9.) Arithmetic Sequences (Linear Functions): In a sequence of numbers, $a_3 = 0, a_4 = 6, a_5 = 12, a_6 = 18$, and $a_7 = 24$.
Based on this information, which equation can be used to find the nth term in the sequence, $a_n$?

$ A.\;\; a_n = -6n + 18 \\[3ex] B.\;\; a_n = -18n + 6 \\[3ex] C.\;\; a_n = 6n - 18 \\[3ex] D.\;\; a_n = 18n - 6 \\[3ex] $

$ \text{3rd term, } a_3 = 0 \\[3ex] \text{4th term, } a_4 = 6 \\[3ex] \text{5th term, } a_5 = 12 \\[3ex] \text{6th term, } a_6 = 18 \\[3ex] \text{7th term, } a_7 = 24 \\[5ex] ..., ..., 0, 6, 12, 18, 24 \\[3ex] 6 - 0 = 6 \\[3ex] 12 - 6 = 6 \\[3ex] 18 - 12 = 6 \\[3ex] 24 - 18 = 6 \\[3ex] $ The sequence is an Arithmetic Sequence because it has a common first difference.

$ \text{common difference,} d = 6 \\[3ex] \text{2nd term, } a_2 = 0 - 6 = -6 \\[3ex] \text{1st term, } a_1 = a = -6 - 6 = -12 \\[3ex] $ We can solve the question using at least two approaches.
Use any approach you prefer.

$ \underline{\text{1st Approach: nth term of an Arithmetic Sequence}} \\[3ex] AS_n = a + d(n - 1) \\[3ex] AS_n = \text{nth term} = a_n \\[3ex] n = \text{number of terms} \\[3ex] \implies \\[3ex] a_n = -12 + 6(n - 1) \\[3ex] a_n = -12 + 6n - 6 \\[3ex] a_n = 6n - 18 \\[3ex] $ For the 2nd Approach, let us represent the information as a linear function.
An Arithmetic Sequence is also known as a Linear Sequence.

Linear Function
x = $n$ y = $a_n$
1 -12
2 -6
3 0
4 6
5 12
6 18
7 24

$ \underline{\text{2nd Approach: Linear Function in Slope–Intercept Form}} \\[3ex] \text{Point 1: } (1, -12) \\[3ex] x_1 = 1 \\[3ex] y_1 = -12 \\[5ex] \text{Point 2: } (7, 24) \\[3ex] x_2 = 7 \\[3ex] y_2 = 24 \\[5ex] \text{Slope, } m = \dfrac{y_2 - y_1}{x_2 - x_1} \\[5ex] m = \dfrac{24 - (-12)}{7 - 1} \\[5ex] m = \dfrac{36}{6} \\[5ex] m = 6 \\[5ex] \text{Point–Slope Form} \\[3ex] y - y_1 = m(x - x_1) \\[3ex] y - (-12) = 6(x - 1) \\[3ex] y + 12 = 6(x - 1) \\[5ex] \text{Slope–Intercept Form} \\[3ex] y = 6(x - 1) - 12 \\[3ex] y = 6x - 6 - 12 \\[3ex] y = 6x - 18 \\[3ex] \implies \\[3ex] a_n = 6n - 18 $
(10.) Variations: The value of y varies directly with x.
If x = 3, then y = 21.
What is the value of x when y = 105?

$ A.\;\; \dfrac{3}{5} \\[5ex] B.\;\; 1\dfrac{2}{3} \\[5ex] C.\;\; 7 \\[3ex] D.\;\; 15 \\[3ex] $

$ y \propto x...\text{Direct Proportion} \\[3ex] y = kx ...k\text{ is the proportionality constant} \\[3ex] \text{If } x = 3, y = 21 \\[3ex] k = ? \\[3ex] 21 = k * 3 \\[3ex] k = \dfrac{21}{3} \\[5ex] k = 7 \\[3ex] \implies \\[3ex] y = 7x \\[5ex] \text{When y = 105}, x = ? \\[3ex] 105 = 7 * x \\[3ex] 7x = 105 \\[3ex] x = \dfrac{105}{7} \\[5ex] x = 15 $

(12.) Linear Functions: A zookeeper recorded the feeding schedule for a baby rhinoceros for 20 weeks.
The table scatterplot show the percentage of the baby rhinoceros's body mass that was used to determine the amount of food given at each feeding as a linear function of its age in weeks.

Baby Rhinoceros Feeding Schedule
Age (weeks) 1 2 4 7 9 12 14 15 17 20
Percentage of Body Mass 20 19.5 17 15 14 13.5 12.4 11.6 11 9



What is the best prediction of the percentage of the body rhinoceros's body mass that should be used to determine the amount of food given at each feeding when it is 25 weeks old?

$ A.\;\; 8.5\% \\[3ex] B.\;\; 6\% \\[3ex] C.\;\; 2.5\% \\[3ex] D.\;\; 10\% \\[3ex] $

$ \underline{\text{Linear Function}} \\[3ex] \text{slope} = m \\[5ex] \text{Point 1: } (1, 20) \\[3ex] x_1 = 1 \\[3ex] y_1 = 20 \\[5ex] \text{Point 2: } (20, 9) \\[3ex] x_2 = 20 \\[3ex] y_2 = 9 \\[5ex] m = \dfrac{y_2 - y_1}{x_2 - x_1} \\[5ex] m = \dfrac{9 - 20}{20 - 1} \\[5ex] m = -\dfrac{11}{19} \\[5ex] \text{Point–Slope Form} \\[3ex] y - y_1 = m(x - x_1) \\[3ex] y - 20 = -\dfrac{11}{19}(x - 1) \\[5ex] y - 20 = -\dfrac{11}{19}x + \dfrac{11}{19} \\[5ex] \text{Slope–Intercept Form} \\[3ex] y = -\dfrac{11}{19}x + \dfrac{11}{19} + 20 \\[5ex] y = -\dfrac{11}{19}x + \dfrac{11}{19} + \dfrac{380}{19} \\[5ex] y = -\dfrac{11}{19}x + \dfrac{391}{19} \\[5ex] \text{When } x = 25 \\[3ex] y = -\dfrac{11}{19} * 25 + \dfrac{391}{19} \\[5ex] y = -\dfrac{275}{19} + \dfrac{391}{19} \\[5ex] y = \dfrac{116}{19} \\[5ex] y = 6.105263158\% $
(13.) Relations and Functions: What are the domain and range of $f(x) = -37$

A. Domain: All real numbers greater than or equal to –37
  Range: All real numbers

B. Domain: {–37}
  Range: All real numbers

C. Domain: All real numbers
  Range: All real numbers greater than or equal to –37

D. Domain: All real numbers
  Range: {–37}


The domain is the set of all the input values, x for which the function has an output.
The range of a function is the set of all output values that result from applying the function to its input values.
The function is a constant function, the output is always –37 regardless of the input.
This implies that:
D. Domain: All real numbers
  Range: {–37}
(14.) Quadratic Functions: The graph of quadratic function p is shown on the grid.



If $k(x) = x^2$ and $p(x) = k(x) + n$, what is the value of n?
Record your answer in the boxes below.




Let us find the graph of p

$ \underline{\text{Equation of a Quadratic Function in Vertex Form}} \\[3ex] p(x) = a(x - h)^2 + k ...\text{where } (h, k) \text{ is the vertex} \\[3ex] (h, k) = (0, -6) \\[3ex] h = 0 \\[3ex] k = -6 \\[3ex] \implies \\[3ex] p(x) = a(x - 0)^2 + -6 \\[3ex] p(x) = ax^2 - 6 \\[5ex] \text{Passes through the point: } (3, 3) \\[3ex] x = 3 \\[3ex] p(x) = 3 \\[3ex] \implies \\[3ex] 3 = a(3)^2 - 6 \\[3ex] 3 = 9a - 6 \\[3ex] 9a - 6 = 3 \\[3ex] 9a = 3 + 6 \\[3ex] 9a = 9 \\[3ex] a = \dfrac{9}{9} \\[5ex] a = 1 \\[5ex] \implies \\[3ex] p(x) = x^2 - 6 \\[5ex] \text{But} \\[3ex] k(x) = x^2 \\[3ex] p(x) = k(x) + n \\[3ex] \implies \\[3ex] x^2 - 6 = x^2 + n \\[5ex] -6 = n \\[3ex] n = -6 $
(15.) System of Linear Equations: Two customers went to a post office to buy postcards and large envelopes.
Each postcard costs the same amount, and each large envelope costs the same amount.
The first customer paid $12 for 14 postcards and 5 large envelopes.
The second customer paid $24.80 for 10 postcards and 15 large envelopes.
What was the cost in dollars of each large envelope?

$ A.\;\; \$1.42 \\[3ex] B.\;\; \$0.35 \\[3ex] C.\;\; \$1.15 \\[3ex] D.\;\; \$0.63 \\[3ex] $

Let the:
cost of a postcard = p
cost of a large envelope = e

The first customer paid $12 for 14 postcards and 5 large envelopes.
⇒ $14p + 5e = 12$

The second customer paid $24.80 for 10 postcards and 15 large envelopes.
⇒ $10p + 15e = 24.8$

$ 14p + 5e = 12 ...eqn.(1) \\[3ex] 10p + 15e = 24.8 ...eqn.(2) \\[5ex] \underline{\text{Elimination Method}} \\[3ex] 5 * eqn.(1) \implies \\[3ex] 5(14p + 5e) = 5(12) \\[3ex] 70p + 25e = 60 ...eqn.(3) \[5ex] 7 * eqn.(2) \implies \\[3ex] 7(10p + 15e) = 7(24.8) \\[3ex] 70p + 105e = 173.6...eqn.(4) \\[5ex] eqn.(4) - eqn.(3) \implies \\[3ex] (70p + 105e) - (70p + 25e) = 173.6 - 60 \\[3ex] 70p + 105e - 70p - 25e = 113.6 \\[3ex] 80e = 113.6 \\[3ex] e = \dfrac{113.6}{80} \\[5ex] e = 1.42 \\[3ex] $ The cost in dollars of each large envelope is $1.42
(16.) Linear Functions: The water level of a river was measured each day during a two-week period.
The graph models the linear relationship between the water level of the river in feet and the number of days the water level was measured.



Which statement best describes the y-intercept of the graph?

A. The water level increased by 0.25 ft per day.
B. The maximum water level was 19.5 ft.
C. The initial water level was 16 ft.
D. The water level was measured for 14 days.


The y-intercept is the point where the graph intersects the y-axis.
At the y-intercept, x = 0
The graph intersects the y-axis at (0, 16)
This implies that: The initial water level was 16 ft.
(17.) Exponential Functions: There are 1,024 players in a tennis tournament.
In each round, half the players are eliminated.
Which function can be used to find the number of players remaining in the tournament at the end of x rounds?

$ A.\;\; f(x) = 1,024(1.50)^x \\[4ex] B.\;\; f(x) = 1,024(0.50)^x \\[4ex] C.\;\; f(x) = 1,024(1.05)^x \\[4ex] D.\;\; f(x) = 1,024(0.05)^x \\[4ex] $

The question is an exponential decay function because: In each round, half the players are eliminated.

$ \underline{\text{Exponential Decay Function}} \\[3ex] f(x) = a(1 - r)^x \\[3ex] a = \text{initial value} = 1024 \\[3ex] r = \text{decay rate} = 50\% = \dfrac{1}{2} = 0.5 \\[5ex] \implies \\[3ex] f(x) = 1024(1 - 0.5)^x \\[3ex] f(x) = 1024(0.5)^x $
(18.) Quadratic Functions: Which statement about $g(x) = x^2 - 576$ is true?

A. The zeros, –288 and 288, can be found when $0 = (x + 288)(x - 288)$.
B. The only zero, 288, can be found when $0 = (x - 288)^2$.
C. The zeros, –24 and 24, can be found when $0 = (x + 24)(x - 24)$.
D. The only zero, 24, can be found when $0 = (x - 24)^2$


$ g(x) = x^2 - 576 \\[3ex] \underline{\text{Zeros of }} g(x) \\[3ex] x^2 - 576 = 0 \\[3ex] x^2 - 24^2 = 0 \\[3ex] (x + 24)(x - 24) = 0 ...\text{Difference of Two Squares} \\[3ex] x + 24 = 0 \text{ or } x - 24 = 0 ...\text{Zero Product Property} \\[3ex] x = -24 \text{ or } x = 24 \\[3ex] $ The correct answer is Option C.
(19.) Linear Inequalities: Which graph best represents the solution set of $-4x \le 6y - 54$

A.

B.

C.

D.


Because the inequality contains an equal sign, the line will be a solid line.

$ -4x \le 6y - 54 \\[5ex] \text{When } x = 0 \\[3ex] -4(0) \le 6y - 54 \\[3ex] 0 \le 6y - 54 \\[3ex] 6y - 54 \ge 0...\text{Swapping LHS and RHS} \\[3ex] 6y \ge 0 + 54 \\[3ex] 6y \ge 54 \\[3ex] y \ge \dfrac{54}{6} \\[5ex] y \gt 9 ...\text{Mark point } (0, 9) \\[3ex] \text{The shaded area is upwards from } y = 9 \\[5ex] \text{When } y = 0 \\[3ex] -4x \le 6(0) - 54 \\[3ex] -4x \le -54 \\[3ex] x \ge \dfrac{-54}{-4}...\text{Division by a negative} \\[5ex] x \ge 13.5 ...\text{Mark point } (13.5, 0) \\[3ex] \text{The shaded area is to the right of } x = 13.5 \\[3ex] $ Draw a straight dashed line connecting the two points: $(0, 9)$ and $(13.5, 0)$
Shade the regions accordingly.
Locate the overlap of the two regions.
The correct answer is Option A.
(20.) Evaluation of Functions: Given $f(x) = \dfrac{1}{3}(4 - x)^2$, what is the value of $f(16)$?
Record your answer in the boxes below.




$ f(x) = \dfrac{1}{3}(4 - x)^2 \\[5ex] f(16) = \dfrac{1}{3} * (4 - 16)^2 \\[5ex] = \dfrac{1}{3} * (-12)^2 \\[5ex] = \dfrac{1}{3} * 144 \\[5ex] = 48 $
(21.) Linear Functions: The graph shows the linear relationship between the maximum area in square feet that can be painted and the number of gallons of paint used.



Which of these best represents the rate of change of the maximum area painted with respect to the number of gallons of paint used?

$ A.\;\; 200ft^2/gal \\[4ex] B.\;\; \dfrac{1}{200}ft^2/gal \\[5ex] C.\;\; 400ft^2/gal \\[4ex] D.\;\; \dfrac{1}{400}ft^2/gal \\[5ex] $

The rate of change of the maximum area painted with respect to the number of gallons of paint used is the slope of the linear function.

$ \text{Point 1: } (0, 0) \\[3ex] x_1 = 0 \\[3ex] y_1 = 0 \\[5ex] \text{Point 2: } (4, 1600) \\[3ex] x_2 = 4 \\[3ex] y_2 = 1600 \\[5ex] \text{Slope, } m = \dfrac{y_2 - y_1}{x_2 - x_1} \\[5ex] m = \dfrac{1600 - 0}{4 - 0} \\[5ex] m = \dfrac{1600}{4} \\[5ex] m = 400 \\[3ex] $ The rate of change of the maximum area painted with respect to the number of gallons of paint used is 400 square feet per gallon.
(22.) Quadratic Equations: What are the solutions to $(x + 7)^2 = 81$?

$ A.\;\; -74 \text{ and } 88 \\[3ex] B,\;\; -2 \text{ and } 16 \\[3ex] C.\;\; -88 \text{ and } 74 \\[3ex] D.\;\; -16 \text{ and } 2 \\[3ex] $

$ (x + 7)^2 = 81 \\[3ex] \text{Square Root Property} \\[3ex] \sqrt{(x + 7)^2} = \pm\sqrt{81} \\[3ex] x + 7 = \pm 9 \\[3ex] x = -7 \pm 9 \\[3ex] x = -7 + 9 \text{ or } x = -7 - 9 \\[3ex] x = 2 \text{ or } x = -16 $
(23.) Exponential Functions: What appears to be the domain of the part of the exponential function graphed on the grid?



$ A.\;\; -1 \le x \le 3 \\[3ex] B.\;\; -1 \le y \le 3 \\[3ex] C.\;\; 5.3 \le x \le 27 \\[3ex] D.\;\; 5.3 \le y \le 27 \\[3ex] $

The domain is the set of all the input values, x for which the function has an output.
The closed circle represents a closed interval. It shows that the endpoint is included.

On the graph:
The closed circle on the left hand side is at x = –1
The closed circle on the right hand side is at x = 3

The interval notation is: [–1, 3]
The set notation is: Domain = $\{x: -1 \le x \le 3 \}$
(24.) System of Linear Equations: The tables of ordered pairs represent some points on the graphs of lines q and v.



Which system of equations is represented by lines q and v?

$ A.\;\; 21x - y = 9 \\[3ex] \hspace{1.6em} 5x + 6y = 40 \\[5ex] B.\;\; 3x - y = -27 \\[3ex] \hspace{1.6em} x + 2y = 16 \\[5ex] C.\;\; 21x - y = 9 \\[3ex] \hspace{1.6em} 5x + 6y = 20 \\[5ex] D.\;\; 9x - y = -27 \\[3ex] \hspace{1.6em} x + 2y = 8 \\[3ex] $

$ \text{slope} = m \\[3ex] y - y_1 = m(x - x_1)...\text{Point–Slope Form} \\[3ex] y = mx + b ...\text{Slope–Intercept Form} \\[3ex] Ax + By = C ...\text{where } A \gt 0 ...\text{Standard Form} \\[5ex] \underline{\text{Line q}} \\[3ex] \text{Point 1: } (-9, 0) \\[3ex] x_1 = -9 \\[3ex] y_1 = 0 \\[5ex] \text{Point 2: } (2, 33) \\[3ex] x_2 = 2 \\[3ex] y_2 = 33 \\[5ex] m = \dfrac{y_2 - y_1}{x_2 - x_1} \\[5ex] m = \dfrac{33 - 0}{2 - (-9)} \\[5ex] m = \dfrac{33}{11} \\[5ex] m = 3 \\[5ex] \text{Point–Slope Form} \\[3ex] y - 0 = 3[x - (-9)] \\[3ex] y = 3(x + 9) \\[5ex] \text{Slope–Intercept Form} \\[3ex] y = 3x + 27 \\[5ex] \text{Standard Form} \\[3ex] -27 = 3x - y \\[3ex] 3x - y = -27 \\[5ex] \underline{\text{Line v}} \\[3ex] \text{Point 1: } (-4, 10) \\[3ex] x_1 = -4 \\[3ex] y_1 = 10 \\[5ex] \text{Point 2: } (10, 3) \\[3ex] x_2 = 10 \\[3ex] y_2 = 3 \\[5ex] m = \dfrac{y_2 - y_1}{x_2 - x_1} \\[5ex] m = \dfrac{3 - 10}{10 - (-4)} \\[5ex] m = \dfrac{-7}{14} \\[5ex] m = -\dfrac{1}{2} \\[5ex] \text{Point–Slope Form} \\[3ex] y - 10 = -\dfrac{1}{2}[x - (-4)] \\[5ex] y - 10 = -\dfrac{1}{2}(x + 4) \\[5ex] y - 10 = -\dfrac{1}{2}x - 2 \\[5ex] \text{Slope–Intercept Form} \\[3ex] y = -\dfrac{1}{2}x - 2 + 10 \\[5ex] y = -\dfrac{1}{2}x + 8 \\[5ex] \text{Standard Form} \\[3ex] \text{LCD} = 2 \\[3ex] 2y = 2\left(-\dfrac{1}{2}x\right) + 2(8) \\[5ex] 2y = -x + 16 \\[3ex] 2y + x = 16 \\[3ex] x + 2y = 16 \\[5ex] \therefore \text{The system of equations shown on the graph is:} \\[3ex] 3x - y = -27 \\[3ex] x + 2y = 16 $
(25.) Correlation and Causation: Which situation does NOT show causation?

A. When the student population at a school increases, the number of teachers at the school increases.
B. When the amount of sugar in a quart of apple juice is reduced, there are fewer calories in each serving.
C. When there are more workers on a project, the project is completed in less time.
D. When there is more protein in an athlete's diet, the athlete scores more points in a game.


Let us analyze each option.
A. When the student population at a school increases, the number of teachers at the school increases.
This shows causation because schools hire more teachers to accommodate more students.

B. When the amount of sugar in a quart of apple juice is reduced, there are fewer calories in each serving.
This is causation because sugar directly contributes calories.

C. When there are more workers on a project, the project is completed in less time.
This is causation because increasing labor typically reduces the time needed to finish the work.

D. When there is more protein in an athlete's diet, the athlete scores more points in a game. This does not show causation.
Eating more protein does not directly cause an athlete to score more points; many other factors such as skills and training among others influence performance.
(26.) Quadratic Functions: Which function is equivalent to $f(x) = -4(x + 7)^2 - 6$?

$ A.\;\; f(x) = -4x^2 - 56x - 202 \\[3ex] B.\;\; f(x) = -4x^2 + 14x + 43 \\[3ex] C,\;\; f(x) = -4x^2 - 56x - 172 \\[3ex] D.\;\; f(x) = -4x^2 + 190 \\[3ex] $

There are at least two approaches that we can use to solve the question.
Use any approach you prefer.

$ \text{1st Approach: Expansion} \\[3ex] f(x) = -4(x + 7)^2 - 6 \\[3ex] = -4[(x + 7)(x + 7)] - 6 \\[3ex] = -4(x^2 + 7x + 7x + 49) - 6 \\[3ex] = -4(x^2 + 14x + 49) - 6 \\[3ex] = -4x^2 - 56x - 196 - 6 \\[3ex] = -4x^2 - 56x - 202 \\[5ex] \text{2nd Approach: Conversion} \\[3ex] f(x) = -4(x + 7)^2 - 6 \\[3ex] \text{Compare to: } f(x) = a(x - h)^2 + k ...\text{Quadratic Function in Vertex Form} \\[3ex] a = -4 \\[3ex] -h = 7 \implies h = -7 \\[3ex] k = -6 \\[3ex] \text{Vertex} = (h, k) = (-7, -6) \\[3ex] x-\text{coordinate of Vertex} = -7 \\[3ex] y-\text{coordinate of Vertex} = -6 \\[5ex] \text{Also} \\[3ex] x-\text{coordinate of Vertex} = -\dfrac{b}{2a} \\[5ex] \implies \\[3ex] -\dfrac{b}{2a} = -7 \\[5ex] \dfrac{b}{2(-4)} = 7 \\[5ex] \dfrac{b}{-8} = 7 \\[5ex] b = 7(-8) \\[3ex] b = -56 \\[5ex] \text{Also} \\[3ex] y-\text{coordinate of Vertex} = \dfrac{4ac - b^2}{4a} \\[5ex] \implies \\[3ex] \dfrac{4ac - b^2}{4a} = -6 \\[5ex] \dfrac{4 \cdot -4 \cdot c - (-56)^2}{4 \cdot -4} = -6 \\[5ex] \dfrac{-16c - 3136}{-16} = -6 \\[5ex] -16c - 3136 = -6 \cdot -16 \\[3ex] -16c = 96 + 3136 \\[3ex] -16c = 3232 \\[3ex] c = \dfrac{3232}{-16} \\[5ex] c = -202 \\[5ex] \text{Convert to: } y = ax^2 + bx + c ...\text{Quadratic Function in Standard Form} \\[3ex] f(x) = -4x^2 - 56x - 202 $
(27.) Linear Functions: A paper airplane was thrown from the top of a tall building.
The height of the paper airplane above the ground can be found using the function $y = -1.5x + 60$, where x is the time in seconds the airplane has been in the air.



How many seconds did it take the paper airplane to reach the ground?
Record your answer in the boxes below.




When the paper airplane reaches the ground, the height is zero.
Hence, to find the time it takes to reach the ground,

$ y = -1.5x + 60 \\[3ex] 0 = -1.5x + 60 \\[3ex] 1.5x = 60 \\[3ex] x = \dfrac{60}{1.5} \\[5ex] x = 40 \\[3ex] $ It takes the paper airplane 40 seconds to reach the ground.

$ A.\;\; y = 6; \text{ slope is } -\dfrac{1}{6}. \\[5ex] B.\;\; x = 6; \text{ slope is zero}. \\[3ex] C.\;\; y = 6; \text{ slope is } 6. \\[3ex] D.\;\; x = 6; \text{ slope is undefined}. \\[3ex] $

Student: SamDom, could you explain why the slope of a vertical line is undefined?
Teacher: Sure.
Let's do it.

$ m = \text{slope} = \dfrac{y_2 - y_1}{x_2 - x_1} \\[5ex] \underline{\text{Vertical Line}} \\[3ex] \text{Point 1: } (6, -8) \\[3ex] x_1 = 6 \\[3ex] y_1 = -8 \\[5ex] \text{Point 2: } (6, 8) \\[3ex] x_2 = 6 \\[3ex] y_2 = 8 \\[5ex] m = \dfrac{8 - (-8)}{6 - 6} \\[5ex] m = \dfrac{16}{0} \\[5ex] m = \text{undefined...division by zero} $
(33.) Exponential Functions: In the year 1900, the total number of metric tons of copper produced in the world was 495,000.
Each year since 1900, the total number of metric tons of copper produced has increased on average by about 3.25% over the amount produced the previous year.
Which function models the total number of metric tons of copper produced in the year that is x years since 1900?

$ A.\;\; c(x) = 495,000(1.0325)^x \\[4ex] B.\;\; c(x) = 495,000(0.9675)^x \\[4ex] C.\;\; c(x) = 495,000x^{1.0325} \\[4ex] D.\;\; c(x) = 495,000x^{0.9675} \\[4ex] $

This is a case of Exponential Growth.
Because: Each year since 1900, the total number of metric tons of copper produced has increased on average by about 3.25% over ...

c(x) = total number of metric tons of copper produced in the year that is x years since 1900.

In the year 1900, the total number of metric tons of copper produced in the world was 495,000.
⇒ the initial value, a = 495,000

Each year since 1900, the total number of metric tons of copper produced has increased on average by about 3.25% over the amount produced the previous year.
⇒ the growth rate, $r = 3.25\% = \dfrac{3.25}{100} = 0.0325$

$ \underline{\text{Exponential Growth Function}} \\[3ex] c(x) = a(1 + r)^x \\[3ex] c(x) = 495000(1 + 0.0325)^x \\[4ex] c(x) = 495000(1.0325)^x $
(34.) Linear Equations: What is the solution to $34x + 95 = 3(14x + 9)$?
Record your answer in the boxes below.




$ 34x + 95 = 3(14x + 9) \\[3ex] 34x + 95 = 42x + 27 \\[3ex] 95 - 27 = 42x - 34x \\[3ex] 68 = 8x \\[3ex] 8x = 68 \\[3ex] x = \dfrac{68}{8} \\[5ex] x = 8.5 $
(35.) Algebra Transformations: The graphs of linear functions f and g are shown on the grid.



Which function is best represented by the graph of g?

$ A.\;\; g(x) = f(x) - 4 \\[3ex] B.\;\; g(x) = \dfrac{1}{3}f(x) \\[5ex] C.\;\; g(x) = f(x) - 2 \\[3ex] D.\;\; g(x) = 3f(x) \\[3ex] $

Let us analyze each option.
Before we do so, let us look for integer coordinates for both graphs f and g
At least two points are sufficient to see a pattern.

Transformation of Functions
Parent Function, $f(x)$ Child (Transformed) Function, $g(x)$
(3, 3) (3, 1)
(6, 6) (6, 2)
We notice that: x-ccordinates are the same.
y-ccordinates change, hence it is a vertical transformation.

$ \dfrac{1}{3} * 3 = 1 \\[5ex] \dfrac{1}{3} * 6 = 2 \\[5ex] \therefore, \dfrac{1}{3} * f(x) = g(x) \\[5ex] g(x) = \dfrac{1}{3}f(x) $
(36.) Multiplication of Polynomials: Which expression is equivalent to $(h^2 + 9h - 1)(-4h + 3)$?

$ A.\;\; -4h^3 - 33h^2 + 31h - 3 \\[4ex] B.\;\; 4h^3 + 39h^2 - 23h - 3 \\[4ex] C.\;\; -4h^3 - 39h^2 + 23h + 3 \\[4ex] D.\;\; 4h^3 + 33h^2 - 31h + 3 \\[4ex] $

$ (h^2 + 9h - 1)(-4h + 3) \\[3ex] h^2 \cdot -4h = -4h^3 \\[3ex] h^2 \cdot 3 = 3h^2 \\[3ex] 9h \cdot -4h = -36h^2 \\[3ex] 9h \cdot 3 = 27h \\[3ex] -1 \cdot -4h = 4h \\[3ex] -1 \cdot 3 = -3 \\[3ex] \implies \\[3ex] -4h^3 + 3h^2 - 36h^2 + 27h + 4h - 3 \\[3ex] -4h^3 - 33h^2 + 31h - 3 $
(37.) System of Linear Equations: There are 15 plates in a kitchen cabinet.
The diameter of each plate is either 7 inches or 12 inches.
The diameter of all 15 plates combined is 140 inches.
Which system of equations can be used to find the number of 7-inch plates, x, and the number of 12-inch plates, y, that are in the cabinet?

$ A.\;\; x + y = 140 \\[3ex] \hspace{1.6em} 12x + 7y = 15 \\[5ex] B.\;\; 7x + 12y = 140 \\[3ex] \hspace{1.6em} 7x + 12y = 15 \\[5ex] C.\;\; x + y = 15 \\[3ex] \hspace{1.6em} 7x + 12y = 140 \\[5ex] D.\;\; x + y = 15 \\[3ex] \hspace{1.6em} 12x + 7y = 140 \\[3ex] $

x = the number of 7-inch plates
y = the number of 12-inch plates

There are 15 plates in a kitchen cabinet.
⇒ $x + y = 15$

Diameter of 7-inch plates = $7x$
Diameter of 12-inch plates = $12y$
The diameter of all 15 plates combined is 140 inches.
⇒ $7x + 12y = 140$
Option C. is the correct answer.
(38.) Quadratic Functions: The graph of quadratic function f is shown on the grid.



Which of these best represents the domain of f?

$ A.\;\; -3 \le x \le 2 \\[3ex] B.\;\; \text{All real numbers} \\[3ex] C.\;\; y \ge 5.5 \\[3ex] D.\;\; \text{All real numbers less than } -3 \text{ or greater than } 2 \\[3ex] $

The domain is the set of all the input values, x for which the function has an output.
The arrow represents infinity (positive or negative infinity as applicable).
On the graph, the domain has arrows on both the LHS (Left Hand Side) and the RHS (Right Hand Side).
This means that the domain includes both positive infinity and negative infinity.
Therefore, the domain is all real numbers.
(39.) Linear Functions: What is the equation in slope–intercept form of the line that passes through the point (2, –2) and is perpendicular to the line represented by $y = \dfrac{2}{5}x + 2$

$ A.\;\; y = \dfrac{5}{2}x - 7 \\[5ex] B.\;\; y = \dfrac{6}{2}x + 7 \\[5ex] C.\;\; y = -\dfrac{5}{2}x - 3 \\[5ex] D.\;\; y = -\dfrac{5}{2}x + 3 \\[5ex] $

$ m = \text{slope} \\[3ex] \text{Point–Slope Form: } y - y_1 = m(x - x_1) \\[3ex] \text{Slope–Intercept Form: } y = mx + b \\[5ex] \underline{\text{Equation 1}} \\[3ex] y = \dfrac{2}{5}x + 2 \\[5ex] m_1 = \dfrac{2}{5} \\[5ex] \underline{\text{Equation 2}} \\[3ex] \text{Line 2 } \perp \text{ Line 1} \\[3ex] m_1 \cdot m_2 = -1 ...\text{The product of the slopes of two perpendicular lines is} -1 \\[3ex] m_2 = -1 \div m_1 \\[3ex] m_2 = -1 \div \dfrac{2}{5} \\[5ex] m_2 = -1 * \dfrac{5}{2} \\[5ex] m_2 = -\dfrac{5}{2} \\[5ex] \text{Passes through the Point } (2, -2) \\[3ex] x_1 = 2 \\[3ex] y_1 = -2 \\[5ex] \text{Point–Slope Form} \\[3ex] y - (-2) = -\dfrac{5}{2}(x - 2) \\[5ex] y + 2 = -\dfrac{5}{2}x + 5 \\[5ex] \text{Slope–Intercept Form} \\[3ex] y = -\dfrac{5}{2}x + 5 - 2 \\[5ex] y = -\dfrac{5}{2}x + 3 $
(40.) Exponential Functions: Which graph best represents $f(x) = 2(5)^x$

A.

B.

C.

D.


$ y = 2(5)^x \\[3ex] \text{Compare to:} \\[3ex] y = ab^x...\text{General Form of an Exponential Function} \\[5ex] a = \text{initial value} = 2 \\[3ex] b = \text{growth factor} = 5 \\[3ex] $ Because the growth factor, 5 is greater than 1, the exponential function is an exponential growth function.
Let us analyze the options.
The initial value is 2.
Discard Option C.
Discard Option D.

$ \text{ When } x = 1 \\[3ex] y = 2(5)^1 \\[3ex] y = 2(5) \\[3ex] y = 10 \\[3ex] $ Discard Option B.
Option A. is the correct answer.
(41.) Quadratic Equations: The area of a rectangular trampoline is 112 ft².
The length of the trampoline is 6 ft greater than the width of the trampoline.
This situation can be represented by the equation $w^2 + 6w - 112 = 0$.
What is the width of the trampoline in feet?

$ A.\;\; 7 \text{ ft} \\[3ex] B.\;\; 16 \text{ ft} \\[3ex] C.\;\; 8 \text{ ft} \\[3ex] D.\;\; 14 \text{ ft} \\[3ex] $

Let the width of the trampoline = w

$ w^2 + 6w - 112 = 0 \\[3ex] \text{Factors are: } 14 \text{ and } -8 \\[3ex] \implies \\[3ex] (w + 14)(w - 8) = 0 w + 14 = 0 \text{ or } w - 8 = 0 ...\text{Zero Product Property} \\[3ex] w = -14 \text{ or } w = 8 \\[3ex] $ The width cannot be negative, hence the width is 8 feet.
(42.) Linear Functions: The table shows the linear relationship between the balance of a student's savings account and the number of weeks he has been saving.

Savings Account
Week 0 1 3 6 8 13
Balance (dollars) 32 39 53 74 88 123

Based on the table, what was the rate of change of the balance of the student's savings account in dollars and cents per week?
Record your answer in the boxes below. Be sure to use the correct place value.




The rate of change of the balance of the student's savings account in dollars and cents per week is the slope of the linear function.

$ \text{Point 1: } (0, 32) \\[3ex] x_1 = 0 \\[3ex] y_1 = 32 \\[5ex] \text{Point 2: } (13, 123) \\[3ex] x_2 = 13 \\[3ex] y_2 = 123 \\[5ex] \text{Slope, } m = \dfrac{y_2 - y_1}{x_2 - x_1} \\[5ex] m = \dfrac{123 - 32}{13 - 0} \\[5ex] m = \dfrac{91}{13} \\[5ex] m = 7 \\[3ex] m = \$7.00 \\[3ex] $ The rate of change of the balance of the student's savings account in dollars and cents per week is 7 dollars and 0 cents per week.
(43.) Linear Functions: The graph of a linear function is shown on the grid.



Which equation is best represented by this graph?

$ A.\;\; y + 7 = -3(x - 4) \\[3ex] B.\;\; y + 1 = -3(x + 2) \\[3ex] C.\;\; y - 4 = 3(x + 7) \\[3ex] D.\;\; y - 2 = 3(x - 1) \\[3ex] $

$ \text{Slope–Intercept Form: } y = mx + b \\[5ex] m = \text{slope} \\[3ex] b = y-\text{intercept} = 5 \\[5ex] \text{Point 1: } (0, 5) \\[3ex] x_1 = 0 \\[3ex] y_1 = 5 \\[5ex] \text{Point 2: } (3, -4) \\[3ex] x_2 = 3 \\[3ex] y_2 = -4 \\[5ex] m = \dfrac{y_2 - y_1}{x_2 - x_1} \\[5ex] m = \dfrac{-4 - 5}{3 - 0} \\[5ex] m = \dfrac{-9}{3} \\[5ex] m = -3 \\[5ex] \text{Slope–Intercept Form} \\[3ex] y = -3x + 5 \\[5ex] \underline{\text{Test Options}} \\[3ex] \text{Option A.} \\[3ex] \text{Add 7 to both sides and factorize} \\[3ex] y + 7 = -3x + 5 + 7 \\[3ex] y + 7 = -3x + 12 \\[3ex] y + 7 = -3(x - 4) \\[3ex] $ Option A. is the correct answer.
(44.) Factoring Quadratic Trinomials: Which expression is a factor of $9r^2 - 4r + 1$?

$ A.\;\; 3r - 1 \\[3ex] B.\;\; r - 1 \\[3ex] C.\;\; 9r - 1 \\[3ex] D.\;\; \text{There are no real factors}. \\[3ex] $

$ 9r^2 - 4r + 1 \\[3ex] 9r^2 \cdot 1 = 9r^2 \\[3ex] \text{Factors are: } ? \\[3ex] $ The trinomial cannot be factored.
Let us confirm by finding the discriminant.

$ \text{Compare to the standard form: } ar^2 + br + c \\[3ex] a = 9 \\[3ex] b = -4 \\[3ex] c = 1 \\[3ex] \text{Discriminant} = b^2 - 4ac \\[3ex] = (-4)^2 - 4(9)(1) \\[3ex] = 16 - 36 \\[3ex] = -20 \\[3ex] $ The discriminant is not a perfect square.
Hence, the trinomial is prime.
(45.) Linear Functions: The graph of $2x - 5y = 10$ is shown on the grid.



Which ordered pair is in the solution set of $2x - 5y \ge 10$?

$ A.\;\; (0, 5) \\[3ex] B.\;\; (5, 0) \\[3ex] C.\;\; (-2, 5) \\[3ex] D.\;\; (-5, 2) \\[3ex] $

There are at least two approaches to solving this question.
Use any approach you prefer.

1st Approach: Algebraic Solution
This involves checking each option to see the one that satisfies the inequality.

$ 2x - 5y \ge 10 \\[5ex] \text{Option A.} \\[3ex] (0, 5) \\[3ex] x = 0 \\[3ex] y = 5 \\[3ex] 2(0) - 5(5) \stackrel{?}{\ge} 10 \\[3ex] 0 - 25 \stackrel{?}{\ge} 10 \\[3ex] -25 \ngeq 10 \\[3ex] \text{Discard}. \\[5ex] \text{Option B.} \\[3ex] (5, 0) \\[3ex] x = 5 \\[3ex] y = 0 \\[3ex] 2(5) - 5(0) \stackrel{?}{\ge} 10 \\[3ex] 10 - 0 \stackrel{?}{\ge} 10 \\[3ex] 10 = 10 \\[3ex] 10 \ge 10 \\[3ex] \text{This is the correct answer}. \\[5ex] \text{Option C.} \\[3ex] (-2, 5) \\[3ex] x = -2 \\[3ex] y = 5 \\[3ex] 2(-2) - 5(5) \stackrel{?}{\ge} 10 \\[3ex] -4 - 25 \stackrel{?}{\ge} 10 \\[3ex] -29 \ngeq 10 \\[3ex] \text{Discard}. \\[5ex] \text{Option D.} \\[3ex] (-5, 2) \\[3ex] x = -5 \\[3ex] y = 2 \\[3ex] 2(-5) - 5(2) \stackrel{?}{\ge} 10 \\[3ex] -10 - 10 \stackrel{?}{\ge} 10 \\[3ex] -20 \ngeq 10 \\[3ex] \text{Discard}. \\[3ex] $ 2nd Approach: Graphical Solution
They gave us a graph, so apparently, they want us to graph the inequality and use that graph in determining the solution.
Because the inequality contains an equal sign, the line will be a solid line.

$ 2x - 5y \ge 10 \\[5ex] \text{When } x = 0 \\[3ex] 2(0) - 5y \ge 10 \\[3ex] 0 - 5y \ge 10 \\[3ex] y \le \dfrac{10}{-5} ...\text{Division by a negative} \\[5ex] y \le -2 ...\text{Point } (0, -2) \\[3ex] \text{The shaded area is downwards from } y = -2 \\[5ex] \text{When } y = 0 \\[3ex] 2x - 5(0) \ge 10 \\[3ex] 2x - 0 \ge 10 \\[3ex] x \ge \dfrac{10}{2} \\[5ex] x \ge 5 ...\text{Point } (5, 0) \\[3ex] \text{The shaded area is to the right of } x = 5 \\[3ex] $ The graph of the inequality is:



An ordered pair in the shaded region is in the solution set of the inequality.
Let us analyze each option.

Option A.
$(0, 5)$ is outside the shaded region.
Discard.

Option B.
$(5, 0)$ is on the solid line.
Because of the equality sign, it is inside the solution set. This is the correct answer.
However, let us analyze the remaining options if you wish.

Option C.
$(-2, 5)$ is outside the shaded region.
Discard.

Option D.
$(-5, 2)$ is outside the shaded region.
Discard.
(46.) Exponential Functions: Scientists are studying a bacteria sample.
The function $f(x) = 245(1.12)^x$ gives the number of bacteria in the sample at the end of x days.
Which statement is the best interpretation of one of the values in this function?

A. The initial number of bacteria is 12.
B. The initial number of bacteria decreases at a rate of 88% each day.
C. The number of bacteria increases at a rate of 12% each day.
D. The number of bacteria at the end of one day is 245.


$ \underline{\text{Exponential Function}} \\[3ex] f(x) = 245(1.12)^x \\[4ex] \text{initial value} = 245 \\[3ex] 1.12 \gt 1 ...\text{hence the function is Exponential Growth} \\[3ex] \text{growth factor} = 1.12 \\[5ex] \underline{\text{Exponential Growth Function}} \\[3ex] f(x) = 245(1 + 0.12)^x \\[4ex] \text{growth rate} = 0.12 * 100 = 12\% \\[3ex] $ This implies that the number of bacteria increases at a rate of 12% each day.
(47.) Relations and Functions: The daily cost of hiring a plumber, y, to work x hours on a repair project can be modeled using a linear function.
The plumber charges a fixed cost of $80 plus an additional cost of $45 per hour.
The plumber works a maximum of 8 hours per day.
For one day of work, what is the range of the function for this situation?

$ A.\;\; 0 \le x \le 8 \\[3ex] B.\;\; 80 \le y \le 440 \\[3ex] C.\;\; 0 \le x \le 10 \\[3ex] D.\;\; 45 \le y \le 685 \\[3ex] $

The range is the set of all the output values, y produced by the input values of the function.

Number of hours on a repair project = x
Daily cost of hiring a plumber = y

x hours @ $45 per hour = $45x$
Fixed cost of $80 ⇒ $y = 80 + 45x$

$ \underline{\text{For one day of work:}} \\[5ex] \text{minimum number of hours} = 0 \\[3ex] y = 80 + 45(0) \\[3ex] y = 80 + 0 \\[3ex] y = \$80 \\[5ex] \text{maximum number of hours} = 8 \\[3ex] y = 80 + 45(8) \\[3ex] y = 80 + 360 \\[3ex] y = \$440 \\[5ex] \text{range of the function is:} \\[3ex] 80 \le y \le 440 $
(48.) Algebra Transformations: The graph of $g(x) = x^2$ was transformed to create the graph of $h(x) = -\left(\dfrac{x}{4}\right)^2$.
Which of these describes the transformation from the graph of g to the graph of h?

A. A reflection over the x-axis and a horizontal stretch.
B. A reflection over the y-axis and a horizontal stretch.
C. A reflection over the x-axis and a vertical stretch.
D. A reflection over the y-axis and a vertical stretch.


Parent Function
$ g(x) = x^2 $

Transformed (Child) Function
$ h(x) = -\left(\dfrac{x}{4}\right)^2 $

1st Transformation: Horizontal stretch by a factor of 4 units.

2nd Transformation: Vertical Reflection (or reflection over the x-axis).
The correct answer is Option A.
(49.) Exponents: Which expression is equivalent to $\dfrac{10q^5w^7}{2w^3} \cdot \dfrac{4(q^6)^2}{w^{-5}}$ for all values of q and w where the expression is defined?

$ A.\;\; \dfrac{32q^7}{w} \\[5ex] B.\;\; 20q^{17}w^9 \\[4ex] C.\;\; 32q^7w^9 \\[4ex] D.\;\; 20qw \\[3ex] $

$ \dfrac{10q^5w^7}{2w^3} \cdot \dfrac{4(q^6)^2}{w^{-5}} \\[5ex] \text{DISSOCIATE and SOLVE} \\[3ex] \dfrac{10 \cdot q^5 \cdot w^7}{2 \cdot w^3} \cdot \dfrac{4 \cdot q^{6 \cdot 2}}{w^{-5}} ...\text{Law 5 Exp} \\[5ex] \dfrac{10 \cdot q^5 \cdot w^7}{2 \cdot w^3} \cdot \dfrac{4 \cdot q^{12}}{w^{-5}} \\[5ex] \dfrac{10 \cdot 4}{2} \cdot q^5 \cdot q^{12} \cdot \dfrac{w^7}{w^3 \cdot w^{-5}} \\[5ex] 20 \cdot q^{5 + 12} \cdot w^{7 - 3 - (-5)} ...\text{Laws 1 and 2 Exp} \\[4ex] 20 \cdot q^{17} \cdot w^{9} \\[4ex] \text{ASSOCIATE} \\[3ex] 20q^{17}w^9 $
(50.) Quadratic Functions: A graph of a quadratic function is shown on the grid.



Which coordinates best represent the vertex of the graph?

$ A.\;\; (2.4, 0) \\[3ex] B.\;\; (0, -1) \\[3ex] C.\;\; (-0.4, 0) \\[3ex] D.\;\; (1, -2) \\[3ex] $

The vertex is the minimum point on the parabola.
The coordinates of the vertex is (1, –2)
(51.) Linear Functions: What is the slope of the line that passes through the points (5, –11) and (–9, 17)?

$ A.\;\; -2 \\[3ex] B.\;\; -\dfrac{1}{2} \\[5ex] C.\;\; 7 \\[3ex] D.\;\; 2 \\[3ex] $

$ \text{Point 1: } (5, -11) \\[3ex] x_1 = 5 \\[3ex] y_1 = -11 \\[5ex] \text{Point 2: } (-9, 17) \\[3ex] x_2 = -9 \\[3ex] y_2 = 17 \\[5ex] \text{Slope, } m = \dfrac{y_2 - y_1}{x_2 - x_1} \\[5ex] m = \dfrac{17 - (-11)}{-9 - 5} \\[5ex] m = \dfrac{28}{-14} \\[5ex] m = -2 $
(52.) System of Linear Equations: What is the x-value of the solution to this system of equations?

$ x = 2y - 4 \\[3ex] 7x + 5y = -66 \\[5ex] A.\;\; -2 \\[3ex] B.\;\; -\dfrac{19}{7} \\[5ex] C.\;\; -8 \\[3ex] D.\;\; -\dfrac{62}{19} \\[5ex] $

$ x = 2y - 4...eqn.(1) \\[3ex] 7x + 5y = -66...eqn.(2) \\[5ex] \underline{\text{Substitution Method}} \\[3ex] \text{From } eqn.(1) \\[3ex] \text{Substitute for } x \text{ in } eqn.(2) \\[3ex] 7(2y - 4) + 5y = -66 \\[3ex] 14y - 28 + 5y = -66 \\[3ex] 19y = -66 + 28 \\[3ex] 19y = -38 \\[3ex] y = -\dfrac{38}{19} \\[5ex] y = -2...eqn.(3) \\[5ex] \text{From } eqn.(3) \\[3ex] \text{Substitute for } y \text{ in } eqn.(1) \\[3ex] x = 2(-2) - 4 \\[3ex] x = -4 - 4 \\[3ex] x = -8 $
(53.) Radicals: Which expression is equivalent to $\sqrt{96}$?

$ A.\;\; 24 \\[3ex] B.\;\; 8\sqrt{6} \\[3ex] C.\;\; 48 \\[3ex] D.\;\; 4\sqrt{6} \\[3ex] $

$ \sqrt{96} \\[3ex] \sqrt{16 \cdot 6} \\[3ex] \sqrt{16} \cdot \sqrt{6} \\[3ex] 4 \cdot \sqrt{6} \\[3ex] 4\sqrt{6} $
